ENDCASE.

ENDFORM.                    " CUSTOMIZE_TOOLBAR_0200
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  CHECK_DATE
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       日付妥当性チェック
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
*      -->P_DAT  日付
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM CHECK_DATE  USING    P_DAT.

CLEAR RC_CODE.
CALL FUNCTION 'CONVERT_DATE_TO_INTERNAL'
EXPORTING
DATE_EXTERNAL            = P_DAT
EXCEPTIONS
DATE_EXTERNAL_IS_INVALID = 1
OTHERS                   = 2.
IF SY-SUBRC <> 0.
RC_CODE = SY-SUBRC.
ENDIF.

ENDFORM.                    " CHECK_DATE
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  CHECK_NUMBER
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       数値妥当性チェック
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
*      -->P_VAL   値
*      <--P_RC    リターンコード
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM CHECK_NUMBER  USING    P_VAL.

DATA: L_VAL(16) TYPE P DECIMALS 5.

CLEAR RC_CODE.
CATCH SYSTEM-EXCEPTIONS CONVT_NO_NUMBER = 1.
L_VAL = P_VAL.
ENDCATCH.
IF SY-SUBRC <> 0.
RC_CODE = SY-SUBRC.
ENDIF.

ENDFORM.                    " CHECK_NUMBER
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  OUTPUT_LOG
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       text
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM OUTPUT_LOG .

DATA: LS_LOGGER LIKE LINE OF T_COMPARE_LOGGER,
LS_COUNTER LIKE LINE OF T_COMPARE_COUNTER.
DATA: L_LINES TYPE I,
L_SKIP TYPE I.
* elematec 対応 2011/12/07 ADD >>>
DATA: LW_POINT_COMPARE   TYPE TYP_POINT_COMPARE.
* elematec 対応 2011/12/22 ADD <<<

IF P_PG = C_ON.
SKIP.
SKIP.
ENDIF.

* タイトルの出力
PERFORM OUTPUT_TITLE.

DESCRIBE TABLE T_COMPARE_LOGGER LINES L_LINES.
IF L_LINES > 0.
WRITE: /04 TEXT-011,                             "会社コード
15 TEXT-012,                             "取引先コード
28 TEXT-013.                             "エラー内容
ULINE.
L_SKIP = 3.
ELSE.
L_SKIP = 1.
ENDIF.

SORT T_COMPARE_LOGGER BY BUKRS VRFCTON.
LOOP AT T_COMPARE_LOGGER INTO LS_LOGGER.
WRITE: /04 LS_LOGGER-BUKRS,                 "会社コード
15 LS_LOGGER-VRFCTON,               "取引先コード
28 LS_LOGGER-MESSAGE.               "エラー内容
ENDLOOP.

DO L_SKIP TIMES.
SKIP.
ENDDO.

DESCRIBE TABLE T_COMPARE_COUNTER LINES L_LINES.
IF L_LINES > 0.
WRITE: /04 TEXT-021,                             "会社コード
15 TEXT-022,                             "取引先コード
30 TEXT-023,                             "照合件数
* elematec 対応 2011/12/07 ADD >>>
*            39 TEXT-024.                             "エラー件数
39  TEXT-025,                            "部分照合件数
56  TEXT-024.                            "エラー件数
* elematec 対応 2011/12/22 ADD <<<
ULINE.
ENDIF.

SORT T_COMPARE_COUNTER BY BUKRS VRFCTON.
LOOP AT T_COMPARE_COUNTER INTO LS_COUNTER.
COUNTER = LS_COUNTER-DIFFERENT_QUANTITY +
LS_COUNTER-DIFFERENT_PRICE +
LS_COUNTER-NO_EXTERNAL +
LS_COUNTER-NO_INTERNAL.
WRITE: /04  LS_COUNTER-BUKRS,                 "会社コード
15  LS_COUNTER-VRFCTON,               "取引先コード
28  LS_COUNTER-OK,                    "照合件数
* elematec 対応 2011/12/07 ADD >>>
*            39  COUNTER.                          "エラー件数
39  LS_COUNTER-POINT_COMPARE,         "部分照合件数
56  COUNTER.                          "エラー件数
* elematec 対応 2011/12/22 ADD <<<
ENDLOOP.
*照合取消　2009/01/21 ADD-S
IF G_CANCEL_NUMBER_10 <> 0 OR G_CANCEL_NUMBER_20 <> 0 .
WRITE: /04 TEXT-021,                             "会社コード
15 TEXT-022,                             "取引先コード
30 TEXT-M31,                             "照合取消件数（外部
52 TEXT-M32.                             "照合取消件数（自社
ULINE.
WRITE: /04 G_BUKRS,                             "会社コード
15 G_VRFCTON,                           "取引先コード
32 G_CANCEL_NUMBER_10,                  "照合取消件数（外部#
54 G_CANCEL_NUMBER_20.                  "照合取消件数（自社#
ENDIF.
*照合取消　2009/01/21 ADD-E

* elematec 対応 2011/12/07 ADD >>>
IF GT_POINT_COMPARE[] IS INITIAL.
ELSE.
SKIP 1.
WRITE: /04 TEXT-021,                             "会社コード
15 TEXT-022,                             "取引先コード
30 TEXT-026.                             "会計伝票番号
ULINE.
ENDIF.
* 部分照合データ画面出力
LOOP AT GT_POINT_COMPARE INTO LW_POINT_COMPARE.
WRITE: /04 LW_POINT_COMPARE-BUKRS,              "会社コード
15 LW_POINT_COMPARE-VRFCTON,            "取引先コード
30 LW_POINT_COMPARE-BELNR.              "会計伝票番号
ENDLOOP.
* elematec 対応 2011/12/22 ADD <<<

ENDFORM.                    " OUTPUT_LOG
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  CHECK_AUTHORITY
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       権限チェック
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
*      -->P_BUKRS  会社コード
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM CHECK_AUTHORITY  USING   P_BUKRS.

DATA: L_OBJECT(10) TYPE C.

CLEAR: RC_CODE.
CASE P_MODE.
WHEN C_MODE_SALES.
L_OBJECT = 'F_KNA1_BUK'.
WHEN C_MODE_PURCHASE.
L_OBJECT = 'F_LFA1_BUK'.
ENDCASE.
AUTHORITY-CHECK OBJECT L_OBJECT
ID 'BUKRS' FIELD P_BUKRS
ID 'ACTVT' DUMMY.
IF SY-SUBRC <> 0.
RC_CODE = C_RC_CODE_NO_AUTHORITY.
ENDIF.

ENDFORM.                    " CHECK_AUTHORITY
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  CHECK_AUTHORITY_RANGE
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       権限チェック
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
*      -->PT_BUKRS  会社コード
*      <--P_EVAL  text
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM CHECK_AUTHORITY_RANGE  TABLES   PT_BUKRS
CHANGING L_EVAL.

DATA: LT_BUKRS LIKE STANDARD TABLE OF T001-BUKRS.
DATA: L_OBJECT(10) TYPE C,
L_BUKRS LIKE T001-BUKRS.

CLEAR: RC_CODE, L_EVAL.
SELECT BUKRS INTO TABLE LT_BUKRS
FROM T001
WHERE BUKRS IN PT_BUKRS.
IF SY-SUBRC <> 0.
* 対象データがありません
RC_CODE = C_RC_CODE_NOT_EXIST.
EXIT.
ENDIF.
CASE P_MODE.
WHEN C_MODE_SALES.
L_OBJECT = 'F_KNA1_BUK'.
WHEN C_MODE_PURCHASE.
L_OBJECT = 'F_LFA1_BUK'.
ENDCASE.
LOOP AT LT_BUKRS INTO L_BUKRS.
AUTHORITY-CHECK OBJECT L_OBJECT
ID 'BUKRS' FIELD L_BUKRS
ID 'ACTVT' DUMMY.
IF SY-SUBRC <> 0.
L_EVAL = L_BUKRS.
RC_CODE = C_RC_CODE_NO_AUTHORITY.
EXIT.
ENDIF.
ENDLOOP.

ENDFORM.                    " CHECK_AUTHORITY_RANGE
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  CHECK_VRFCTON_RANGE
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       取引先コード存在チェック
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
*      -->PT_VRFCTON  取引先コード
*      <--P_EVAL  text
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM CHECK_VRFCTON_RANGE  TABLES   PT_VRFCTON
CHANGING P_EVAL.

FIELD-SYMBOLS: <FS1>, <FS2>, <FS3>.

CLEAR: RC_CODE, P_EVAL.
LOOP AT PT_VRFCTON.
ASSIGN COMPONENT 1 OF STRUCTURE PT_VRFCTON TO <FS1>.
ASSIGN COMPONENT 2 OF STRUCTURE PT_VRFCTON TO <FS2>.
CHECK <FS1> = 'I' AND <FS2> = 'EQ'.
ASSIGN COMPONENT 3 OF STRUCTURE PT_VRFCTON TO <FS3>.
* elematec 対応 2011/12/07 ADD >>>
IF <FS3> CA '*'.              "*が含まれている場合
IF P_MODE = C_MODE_SALES.
MESSAGE E912 WITH TEXT-049.
ELSE.
MESSAGE E902.
ENDIF.
ENDIF.
* elematec 対応 2011/12/07 ADD <<<
PERFORM CHECK_VRFCTON  USING <FS3>.
IF RC_CODE <> 0.
P_EVAL = <FS3>.
EXIT.
ENDIF.
ENDLOOP.
* elematec 対応 2011/12/07 ADD >>>
IF  SY-SUBRC <> 0            "未入力の場合
AND SY-UCOMM+0(1) <> '%'.    "複数入力ボタン押下以外
IF P_MODE = C_MODE_SALES.  "[売上照合]
MESSAGE E901 WITH TEXT-049.
ELSE.                      "[仕入照合]
MESSAGE E901 WITH TEXT-050.
ENDIF.
ENDIF.
* elematec 対応 2011/12/07 ADD <<<

ENDFORM.                    " CHECK_VRFCTON_RANGE
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  CHECK_VRFCTON
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       取引先コード存在チェック
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
*      -->P_VRFCTON  取引先コード存在チェック
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM CHECK_VRFCTON  USING    P_VRFCTON.
* elematec 対応 2011/12/07 ADD >>>
DATA:L_VRFCTON    TYPE CHAR10.

L_VRFCTON = P_VRFCTON.
* elematec 対応 2011/12/07 ADD <<<

**INSERT 20061031 HATTORI
*  CALL FUNCTION 'CONVERSION_EXIT_ALPHA_INPUT'
*       EXPORTING
*            INPUT  = P_VRFCTON
*       IMPORTING
*            OUTPUT = P_VRFCTON.
**INSERT END
* elematec 対応 2011/12/07 ADD >>>
CALL FUNCTION 'CONVERSION_EXIT_ALPHA_INPUT'
EXPORTING

FORM SET_T_ALV_CHECKER_0200 .

DATA: LS_CHECKER LIKE LINE OF T_ALV_CHECKER_0200,

ENDIF.
IF NOT LH_GRID_DATA-YNKNUNTPRC IS INITIAL.
LS_CHECKER-YNKNUNTPRC(21) = LH_GRID_DATA-YNKNUNTPRC. " 単価
ENDIF.
IF NOT LH_GRID_DATA-YNKNTAXAMT IS INITIAL.
LS_CHECKER-YNKNTAXAMT(21) = LH_GRID_DATA-YNKNTAXAMT. " 消費税額
ENDIF.
IF NOT LH_GRID_DATA-YNKNITXAMT IS INITIAL.
LS_CHECKER-YNKNITXAMT(21) = LH_GRID_DATA-YNKNITXAMT. " 税抜金額
ENDIF.
IF NOT LH_GRID_DATA-YNKNETXAMT IS INITIAL.
LS_CHECKER-YNKNETXAMT(21) = LH_GRID_DATA-YNKNETXAMT. " 税込金額
ENDIF.
LS_CHECKER-YNWAERS = LH_GRID_DATA-YNWAERS.    " 通貨コード
* elematec 対応 2011/12/07 ADD >>>
IF NOT LH_GRID_DATA-YNDVSON IS INITIAL.

ENDIF.
IF NOT LH_GRID_DATA-YNLIST2 IS INITIAL.
LS_CHECKER-YNLIST2 = LH_GRID_DATA-YNLIST2.     " 発注伝票

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  CHANGE_T_ALV_CHECKER_0200
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       チェック項目の内容更新
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
*      -->P_OBJ_DATA_CHANGED  更新された項目内容
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM CHANGE_T_ALV_CHECKER_0200
USING P_OBJ_DATA_CHANGED TYPE REF TO CL_ALV_CHANGED_DATA_PROTOCOL.

DATA: LS_CELL TYPE LVC_S_MODI,
LS_ROID TYPE LVC_S_ROID,
LS_LINE TYPE LVC_S_MOCE.
DATA: LS_CHECKER LIKE LINE OF T_ALV_CHECKER_0200,
L_LINNO LIKE SY-TABIX.

FIELD-SYMBOLS: <FS_CHECKER> LIKE LINE OF T_ALV_CHECKER_0200.
FIELD-SYMBOLS: <FS>.

* 行追加
LOOP AT P_OBJ_DATA_CHANGED->MT_INSERTED_ROWS INTO LS_LINE.
CLEAR LS_CHECKER.
LS_CHECKER-ROW_ID = LS_LINE-ROW_ID.
APPEND LS_CHECKER TO T_ALV_CHECKER_0200.
ENDLOOP.

* 行削除
LOOP AT P_OBJ_DATA_CHANGED->MT_DELETED_ROWS INTO LS_LINE.
* elematec 対応 2011/12/07 ADD >>>
* 行削除ボタン時の削除対象レコード修正
*    DELETE T_ALV_CHECKER_0200 INDEX LS_LINE-ROW_ID.
DELETE T_ALV_CHECKER_0200 WHERE ROW_ID =  LS_LINE-ROW_ID.
* elematec 対応 2011/12/07 ADD <<<
ENDLOOP.

* 内容更新
LOOP AT P_OBJ_DATA_CHANGED->MT_MOD_CELLS INTO LS_CELL.
READ TABLE T_ALV_CHECKER_0200 ASSIGNING <FS_CHECKER>
WITH KEY ROW_ID = LS_CELL-ROW_ID.
IF SY-SUBRC = 0.
ASSIGN COMPONENT LS_CELL-FIELDNAME OF STRUCTURE <FS_CHECKER>
TO <FS>.
IF SY-SUBRC = 0.
<FS> = LS_CELL-VALUE.
TRANSLATE <FS> TO UPPER CASE.
ENDIF.
ENDIF.
ENDLOOP.

* 行番更新
LOOP AT P_OBJ_DATA_CHANGED->MT_ROID_FRONT INTO LS_ROID.
L_LINNO = SY-TABIX.
READ TABLE T_ALV_CHECKER_0200 ASSIGNING <FS_CHECKER>
WITH KEY ROW_ID = LS_ROID-ROW_ID.
IF SY-SUBRC = 0.
<FS_CHECKER>-LINNO = L_LINNO.
ENDIF.
ENDLOOP.

* elematec 対応 2011/12/07 ADD >>>
* 行追加ボタン＋エラー時の行指定修正
SORT T_ALV_CHECKER_0200 BY LINNO ROW_ID.
* elematec 対応 2011/12/07 ADD <<<

* elematec 対応 2011/12/07 ADD >>>
* 通貨内部換算
DATA:LW_AMOUNT(8)      TYPE P DECIMALS 2,
LW_AMOUNT_INT(8)  TYPE P DECIMALS 2,
LW_TYPE           TYPE DATATYPE_D,
LW_CHANGE_CURRENT TYPE TYP_CHANGE_CURRENT,
LW_DONE_ROW_ID    TYPE SY-TABIX,
LS_CELL2          TYPE LVC_S_MODI,
LT_CELL2          TYPE STANDARD TABLE OF LVC_S_MODI,
LW_MAKE_CHANGE_DATA TYPE CHAR01,
LW_VALUE          TYPE LVC_VALUE.
TYPES:LTYP_GRID_DATA_0200 TYPE STANDARD TABLE OF TYP_GRID_DATA_0200.
FIELD-SYMBOLS:<F_GRID_0200>  TYPE LTYP_GRID_DATA_0200, "内部テーブル
<FL_GRID_0200> TYPE TYP_GRID_DATA_0200.  "構造
*** 2012/07/12 INSERT START *** 変数定義
DATA LW_LIFNR TYPE CHAR10.
*** 2012/07/12 INSERT END ***

*  CLEAR:T_CHANGE_CURRENT.
* 入力した際に通貨コード"JPY"にもかかわらず、内部テーブルの値が
* 円内部換算されないため
* 金額項目が入力された場合に通貨変数から値を入れなおす
ASSIGN TABLE FIELD
P_OBJ_DATA_CHANGED->MP_MOD_ROWS->* TO <F_GRID_0200>.

LOOP AT <F_GRID_0200> ASSIGNING <FL_GRID_0200>.
*   変更データのうち、消費税額/税抜金額が処理対象
LOOP AT P_OBJ_DATA_CHANGED->MT_MOD_CELLS INTO LS_CELL.
*     最初の1回目
IF LW_DONE_ROW_ID IS INITIAL.
LW_DONE_ROW_ID = LS_CELL-ROW_ID.
ENDIF.
*     処理済のROW_ID
IF LW_DONE_ROW_ID > LS_CELL-ROW_ID.
CONTINUE.
ENDIF.
*     次のレコードのROW_ID
IF LW_DONE_ROW_ID < LS_CELL-ROW_ID.
LW_DONE_ROW_ID = LS_CELL-ROW_ID.   "ローカル変数にROW_ID退避
EXIT.
ENDIF.
*---  税額と税抜金額が変更された場合
IF LS_CELL-FIELDNAME = 'YNKNTAXAMT'
OR LS_CELL-FIELDNAME = 'YNKNITXAMT'.

*       入力された値が数値かどうかのチェックを行う
TRANSLATE LS_CELL-VALUE USING ', '.    "カンマは削除
CONDENSE LS_CELL-VALUE NO-GAPS.
LW_VALUE = LS_CELL-VALUE.
TRANSLATE LW_VALUE USING '- '.    "符号は削除
CALL FUNCTION 'NUMERIC_CHECK'
EXPORTING
STRING_IN = LW_VALUE
IMPORTING
HTYPE     = LW_TYPE.
IF LW_TYPE = 'NUMC'.
*         画面入力の通貨で内部換算する
READ TABLE P_OBJ_DATA_CHANGED->MT_MOD_CELLS
WITH KEY ROW_ID    = LW_DONE_ROW_ID
FIELDNAME = 'YNWAERS'
TRANSPORTING NO FIELDS.
*         通貨コードの変更がある場合はそのまま設定(下記にて処理を行う)
IF SY-SUBRC = 0.
LW_AMOUNT_INT = LS_CELL-VALUE.
*         通貨コードの変更がない場合は内部換算
ELSE.
LW_AMOUNT = LS_CELL-VALUE.
PERFORM CURRENCY_INTERNAL USING <FL_GRID_0200>-YNWAERS
LW_AMOUNT
CHANGING LW_AMOUNT_INT.
ENDIF.
*         ALVデータの最新情報に更新
*         [消費税額]
IF LS_CELL-FIELDNAME = 'YNKNTAXAMT'.
<FL_GRID_0200>-YNKNTAXAMT = LW_AMOUNT_INT.
ENDIF.
*         [税抜金額]
IF LS_CELL-FIELDNAME = 'YNKNITXAMT'.
<FL_GRID_0200>-YNKNITXAMT = LW_AMOUNT_INT.
ENDIF.
ENDIF.
ENDIF.

*---  通貨コードが変更された場合
IF LS_CELL-FIELDNAME = 'YNWAERS'.
CLEAR:LW_MAKE_CHANGE_DATA.
READ TABLE P_OBJ_DATA_CHANGED->MT_MOD_CELLS
WITH KEY ROW_ID    = LW_DONE_ROW_ID
FIELDNAME = 'YNKNTAXAMT'
TRANSPORTING NO FIELDS.
IF SY-SUBRC <> 0.
READ TABLE P_OBJ_DATA_CHANGED->MT_MOD_CELLS
WITH KEY ROW_ID    = LW_DONE_ROW_ID
FIELDNAME = 'YNKNITXAMT'
TRANSPORTING NO FIELDS.
IF SY-SUBRC <> 0.
LW_MAKE_CHANGE_DATA = C_ON.
ENDIF.
ENDIF.

*       [消費税額]
LW_AMOUNT = <FL_GRID_0200>-YNKNTAXAMT.
PERFORM CURRENCY_INTERNAL USING <FL_GRID_0200>-YNWAERS
LW_AMOUNT
CHANGING LW_AMOUNT_INT.
<FL_GRID_0200>-YNKNTAXAMT = LW_AMOUNT_INT.
*        IF LW_MAKE_CHANGE_DATA = C_ON.
*          LS_CELL2 = LS_CELL.
*          LS_CELL2-FIELDNAME = 'YNKNTAXAMT'.
*          LS_CELL2-VALUE = LW_AMOUNT_INT.
*          CONDENSE LS_CELL2-VALUE NO-GAPS.
*          APPEND LS_CELL2 TO LT_CELL2.
*        ENDIF.
*       [税抜金額]
LW_AMOUNT = <FL_GRID_0200>-YNKNITXAMT.
PERFORM CURRENCY_INTERNAL USING <FL_GRID_0200>-YNWAERS
LW_AMOUNT
CHANGING LW_AMOUNT_INT.
<FL_GRID_0200>-YNKNITXAMT = LW_AMOUNT_INT.
ENDIF.
ENDLOOP.
ENDLOOP.
*  APPEND LINES OF LT_CELL2 TO P_OBJ_DATA_CHANGED->MT_MOD_CELLS.
*  APPEND LINES OF LT_CELL2 TO P_OBJ_DATA_CHANGED->MT_GOOD_CELLS.
* elematec 対応 2011/12/07 ADD <<<

ENDFORM.                    " CHANGE_T_ALV_CHECKER_0200

CHANGING <FS_GRID_DATA>-YNPRCTRNAME.

<FS_GRID_DATA>-YNDVSONNAME.

CHANGING <FS_GRID_DATA>-YNDVSONNAME.
ENDIF.

CHANGING <FS_GRID_DATA>-YNLIST1NAME.
* elematec 対応 2011/12/07 ADD <<<
ENDLOOP.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  CHECK_OVERFLOW
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       text
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
*      -->P_FIELDNAME   text
*      -->P_NUMBER  text
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM CHECK_OVERFLOW  USING    P_FIELDNAME
P_NUMBER.

DATA: LS_FCAT LIKE LINE OF T_FCAT_0200.
DATA: L_LEN TYPE I,
L_DEC TYPE I,
L_MAX TYPE STRING.
DATA: L_ABS(21) TYPE C.

CLEAR RC_CODE.
READ TABLE T_FCAT_0200 INTO LS_FCAT
WITH KEY FIELDNAME = P_FIELDNAME.
IF SY-SUBRC = 0.
L_DEC = LS_FCAT-DECIMALS.
L_LEN = LS_FCAT-DD_OUTLEN.
DO L_LEN TIMES.
CONCATENATE L_MAX '9' INTO L_MAX.
ENDDO.
IF L_DEC > 0.
CONCATENATE L_MAX '.' INTO L_MAX.
SHIFT L_MAX BY L_DEC PLACES LEFT CIRCULAR.
ENDIF.
L_ABS = ABS( P_NUMBER ).
IF L_ABS > L_MAX.
RC_CODE = C_RC_CODE_ERROR.
ENDIF.
ENDIF.

ENDFORM.                    " CHECK_OVERFLOW
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  SET_SPECIAL_CHAR
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       text
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM SET_SPECIAL_CHAR USING P_ASCII
CHANGING P_CHAR.

DATA: L_X(4) TYPE X.

FIELD-SYMBOLS: <FS> TYPE C.
L_X = P_ASCII.
ASSIGN L_X TO <FS> CASTING TYPE C.
MOVE <FS>+3(1) TO P_CHAR.

ENDFORM.                    " SET_SPECIAL_CHAR

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  EXECUTE_USER_COMMAND_0200
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       text
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
*      -->P_UCOMM  text
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM EXECUTE_USER_COMMAND_0200 USING    P_UCOMM.

DATA: LS_GRID_DATA LIKE LINE OF T_GRID_DATA_0200.
DATA: LS_ROW TYPE LVC_S_ROW.

CASE P_UCOMM.
WHEN C_USER_COMMAND_COPY_ROW.
CALL METHOD OBJ_GRID_0200->GET_CURRENT_CELL
IMPORTING ES_ROW_ID = LS_ROW.
IF LS_ROW-INDEX > 0.
READ TABLE T_GRID_DATA_0200 INTO LS_GRID_DATA
INDEX LS_ROW-INDEX.
IF SY-SUBRC = 0.
APPEND LS_GRID_DATA TO T_GRID_DATA_0200.
CALL METHOD OBJ_GRID_0200->REFRESH_TABLE_DISPLAY.
CALL METHOD CL_GUI_CFW=>FLUSH.
ENDIF.
ENDIF.
ENDCASE.

ENDFORM.                    " EXECUTE_USER_COMMAND_0200

APPEND P_BUKRS2.

CLEAR:P_DVSON1,P_DVSON2.

CASE SY-TCODE.
WHEN 'ZN04'
OR 'ZN69'
OR 'ZN70'
OR 'ZN71'
OR 'ZN72'
OR 'ZN73'. "仕入照合

OR 'ZN74'
OR 'ZN75'
OR 'ZN76'
OR 'ZN77'
OR 'ZN78'. "売上照合

P_DVSON1-LOW = LW_VKBUR.
WHEN OTHERS.
ENDCASE.
IF NOT P_DVSON1-LOW IS INITIAL.
P_DVSON1-SIGN   = 'I'.
P_DVSON1-OPTION = 'EQ'.
APPEND P_DVSON1.
P_DVSON2 = P_DVSON1.
APPEND P_DVSON2.

APPEND P_DVSON3.
*** 2012/03/07 INSERT END ***
ENDIF.
* 2012/03/05 ADD END

ENDFORM.                    " INIT_OUT

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  CHECK_CZFBDT
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       照合締日の入力値チェック
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
*      -->P_VRFCT1         得意先/仕入先コード
*      -->P_CZFBDT         照合締日
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM CHECK_CZFBDT TABLES   P_VRFCT1
USING    P_CZFBDT TYPE ZNECZFBDT.
* 内部テーブル/構造定義
DATA: LT_ZN001    TYPE STANDARD TABLE OF TYP_ZN001,
LW_ZN001    TYPE TYP_ZN001,
LT_WYT3     TYPE STANDARD TABLE OF TYP_WYT3,
LW_WYT3     TYPE TYP_WYT3,
LT_ZN004    TYPE STANDARD TABLE OF TYP_ZN004,
LW_ZN004    TYPE TYP_ZN004,
LT_KNVP     TYPE STANDARD TABLE OF TYP_KNVP,
LW_KNVP     TYPE TYP_KNVP.
DATA:LW_LINES     TYPE I,
LW_ZFBDT     TYPE ZFBDT,    "今回締日
LW_ZFBDT_OLD TYPE ZFBDT,    "前回締日
LW_CZFBDT    TYPE ZNECZFBDT, "照合締日
*** 2012/03/07 INSERT START ４***
LW_CHECK     TYPE ZFBDT,     "チェック用
*** 2012/03/07 INSERT END ４***
LW_MESSAGE TYPE CHAR10.
DATA:LT_T052 TYPE STANDARD TABLE OF TYP_T052,
LW_T052 TYPE TYP_T052.

*--- 画面;照合締日の退避
IF P_CZFBDT IS INITIAL.
* 2012/04/09 MOD START
*    LW_CZFBDT = '99991231'.
*-- 照合締日が未入力の場合、まず提案値を作成
READ TABLE P_LIST11 INDEX 1.
CLEAR:LW_ZFBDT,LW_ZFBDT_OLD.
IF P_PRCHS = C_ON.          "[仕入照合]
CALL FUNCTION 'YK_ZFBDT_GET_BY_LFM1'
EXPORTING
I_CORD               = P_LIST11-LOW
I_EKORG              = P_EKORG
I_DAY                = SY-DATUM
IMPORTING
E_ZFBDT              = LW_ZFBDT
E_ZFBDT_OLD          = LW_ZFBDT_OLD
EXCEPTIONS
NO_GET_T052          = 1
NO_GOOD_GETDAY       = 2
NO_GET_ZTERM         = 3
OTHERS               = 4.
ELSE.                       "
CALL FUNCTION 'YK_ZFBDT_GET_BY_KNVV'
EXPORTING
I_CORD               = P_LIST11-LOW
I_VKORG              = P_VKORG
I_VTWEG              = P_VTWEG
I_SPART              = P_SPART
I_DAY                = SY-DATUM
IMPORTING
E_ZFBDT              = LW_ZFBDT
E_ZFBDT_OLD          = LW_ZFBDT_OLD
EXCEPTIONS
NO_GET_T052          = 1
NO_GOOD_GETDAY       = 2
NO_GET_ZTERM         = 3
OTHERS               = 4.
ENDIF.
P_CZFBDT = LW_ZFBDT_OLD.
LW_CZFBDT = P_CZFBDT.
* 2012/04/09 MOD END
ELSE.
LW_CZFBDT = P_CZFBDT.
ENDIF.

*--- 仕入照合処理の場合
IF P_PRCHS = C_ON.          "[仕入照合]

*   請求先の取得
SELECT LIFNR                      "発注先
LIFN2                      "請求先
INTO TABLE LT_WYT3
FROM WYT3
WHERE LIFNR IN P_VRFCT1          "発注先
AND EKORG = P_EKORG
*** 2012/03/07 MOD START ３***
*       AND PARVW = P_PARVW.           "請求先
AND LTSNR = SPACE              "仕入先部門
AND WERKS = SPACE              "プラント
AND PARVW = P_PARVW            "請求先取引先機能
AND PARZA = '000'.
*** 2012/03/07 MOD END ３***
LW_WYT3-LIFNR = '+'.
LW_WYT3-LIFN2 = '+'.
APPEND LW_WYT3 TO LT_WYT3.

*   照合期間（仕入）データ取得
SELECT LIFNR
EDATE
INTO TABLE LT_ZN001
FROM ZN001
FOR ALL ENTRIES IN LT_WYT3
WHERE LIFNR = LT_WYT3-LIFN2.
IF SY-SUBRC = 0.
SORT LT_ZN001.
*     入力された仕入先の照合終了日と照合締日をチェック
LOOP AT LT_WYT3 INTO LW_WYT3.
IF LW_WYT3-LIFN2 = '+'.
CONTINUE.
ENDIF.
READ TABLE LT_ZN001 INTO LW_ZN001
WITH KEY LIFNR = LW_WYT3-LIFN2
BINARY SEARCH.
IF SY-SUBRC <> 0.
READ TABLE LT_ZN001 INTO LW_ZN001
WITH KEY LIFNR = '+'
BINARY SEARCH.
ENDIF.
*       すでに照合が終了(同日も終了とする)している場合エラー
*       画面が初期値の場合はMAX日付とチェックするので、エラーとならない
IF LW_CZFBDT <= LW_ZN001-EDATE.
MESSAGE E906 WITH LW_WYT3-LIFNR.
ENDIF.
ENDLOOP.
ENDIF.

*---入力された照合締日の日付と支払条件の締め日付が一致しているかチェック
*   発注先の支払条件と支払条件の期日を取得
SELECT LFM1~LIFNR                 "発注先
LFM1~ZTERM                 "支払条件
T052~ZTAGG                 "期限
INTO TABLE LT_T052
FROM LFM1 INNER JOIN T052
ON LFM1~ZTERM = T052~ZTERM
FOR ALL ENTRIES IN LT_WYT3
WHERE LFM1~LIFNR = LT_WYT3-LIFNR   "発注先
AND LFM1~EKORG = P_EKORG.

*   入力された仕入先の支払条件(締め日付)が一致するかどうかチェック
IF SY-SUBRC = 0.
SORT LT_T052.    "すべてを昇順ソート
*     期限->値が小さいほうを残し削除
DELETE ADJACENT DUPLICATES FROM LT_T052
COMPARING LIFNR ZTERM.
SORT LT_T052 BY ZTAGG.
*     期限の重複を削除
DELETE ADJACENT DUPLICATES FROM LT_T052
COMPARING ZTAGG.
DESCRIBE TABLE LT_T052 LINES LW_LINES.
*     締め日付が複数ある場合はエラー
IF LW_LINES > 1.
MESSAGE E999(YN01) WITH TEXT-052
SPACE
SPACE
SPACE.
ENDIF.

READ TABLE LT_T052 INTO LW_T052 INDEX 1.
IF P_CZFBDT IS INITIAL.
CALL FUNCTION 'YK_ZFBDT_GET_BY_LFM1'
EXPORTING
I_CORD               = LW_T052-LIFNR
I_EKORG              = P_EKORG
I_DAY                = SY-DATUM
IMPORTING
E_ZFBDT              = LW_ZFBDT
E_ZFBDT_OLD          = LW_ZFBDT_OLD
EXCEPTIONS
NO_GET_T052          = 1
NO_GOOD_GETDAY       = 2
NO_GET_ZTERM         = 3
OTHERS               = 4.
*** 2012/03/07 MOD START ４***
*        P_CZFBDT = LW_ZFBDT.
P_CZFBDT = LW_ZFBDT_OLD.
LW_CHECK = LW_ZFBDT_OLD.
*** 2012/03/07 MOD END ４***
ELSE.
*       入力された照合締日と仕入先の締日日付が一致するかどうかチェック
CALL FUNCTION 'YK_ZFBDT_GET_BY_LFM1'
EXPORTING
I_CORD               = LW_T052-LIFNR
I_EKORG              = P_EKORG
I_DAY                = P_CZFBDT
IMPORTING

E_ZFBDT_OLD          = LW_ZFBDT_OLD
EXCEPTIONS
NO_GET_T052          = 1
NO_GOOD_GETDAY       = 2
NO_GET_ZTERM         = 3
OTHERS               = 4.
*** 2012/03/07 INSERT START ４***
LW_CHECK = LW_ZFBDT.
*** 2012/03/07 INSERT END ４***
ENDIF.
*     仕入先締日から算出した締日と、照合締日が不一致の場合はエラー
IF SY-SUBRC = 0.
*** 2012/03/07 MOD START ４***
*        IF LW_ZFBDT <> P_CZFBDT.
IF LW_CHECK <> P_CZFBDT.
*** 2012/03/07 MOD END ４***
*** 2012/03/07 MOD START ５***
*          WRITE LW_ZFBDT TO LW_MESSAGE.
*          MESSAGE E999(YN01) WITH TEXT-054 LW_MESSAGE
*                                  TEXT-055 SPACE.
MESSAGE E913(YN01).
*** 2012/03/07 MOD END ５***
ELSE.
*         請求日/入庫日が初期値の場合は初期値提案
IF P_LDAT11[] IS INITIAL.
P_LDAT11-SIGN   = 'I'.
P_LDAT11-OPTION = 'BT'.
* 2012/03/05 MOD START
* LOW値は提案不要
*            P_LDAT11-LOW    = LW_ZFBDT_OLD + 1.
CLEAR P_LDAT11-LOW.
* 2012/03/05 MOD END
*** 2012/03/07 MOD START ４***
*            P_LDAT11-HIGH   = LW_ZFBDT.
P_LDAT11-HIGH   = LW_CHECK.
*** 2012/03/07 MOD END ４***
APPEND P_LDAT11.
ENDIF.
IF P_LDAT12[] IS INITIAL.
P_LDAT12-SIGN   = 'I'.
P_LDAT12-OPTION = 'BT'.
* 2012/03/05 MOD START
* LOW値は提案不要
*            P_LDAT12-LOW    = LW_ZFBDT_OLD + 1.
CLEAR: P_LDAT12-LOW.
* 2012/03/05 MOD END
*** 2012/03/07 MOD START ４***
*            P_LDAT12-HIGH   = LW_ZFBDT.
P_LDAT12-HIGH   = LW_CHECK.
*** 2012/03/07 MOD END ４***
APPEND P_LDAT12.
ENDIF.
ENDIF.
ENDIF.

ENDIF.

*--- 売上照合処理の場合
ELSE.
*   支払人の取得
SELECT KUNNR                  "受注先
KUNN2                  "支払人
INTO TABLE LT_KNVP
FROM KNVP
WHERE KUNNR IN P_LIST11      "受注先
AND VKORG = P_VKORG
AND VTWEG = P_VTWEG
AND SPART = P_SPART
AND PARVW = P_PARVWK       "支払人
*** 2012/03/07 MOD START ３***
*       AND PARZA = SPACE.
AND PARZA = '000'.
*** 2012/03/07 MOD END ３***
LW_KNVP-KUNNR = '+'.
LW_KNVP-KUNN2 = '+'.
APPEND LW_KNVP TO LT_KNVP.

*   照合期間（売上）データ取得
SELECT KUNNR
EDATE
INTO TABLE LT_ZN004
FROM ZN004
FOR ALL ENTRIES IN LT_KNVP
WHERE KUNNR = LT_KNVP-KUNN2.
IF SY-SUBRC = 0.
SORT LT_ZN004.
*     入力された得意先の照合終了日と照合締日をチェック
LOOP AT LT_KNVP INTO LW_KNVP.
IF LW_KNVP-KUNNR = '+'.
CONTINUE.
ENDIF.
READ TABLE LT_ZN004 INTO LW_ZN004
WITH KEY KUNNR = LW_KNVP-KUNN2
BINARY SEARCH.
IF SY-SUBRC <> 0.
READ TABLE LT_ZN004 INTO LW_ZN004
WITH KEY KUNNR = '+'
BINARY SEARCH.
ENDIF.
*       すでに照合が終了(同日も終了とする)している場合エラー
IF LW_CZFBDT <= LW_ZN004-EDATE.
MESSAGE E916 WITH LW_KNVP-KUNNR.
ENDIF.
ENDLOOP.
ENDIF.

*---入力された照合締日の日付と支払条件の締め日付が一致しているかチェック
*   得意先の支払条件と支払条件の期日を取得
SELECT KNVV~KUNNR                 "支払先
KNVV~ZTERM                 "支払条件
T052~ZTAGG                 "期限
INTO TABLE LT_T052
FROM KNVV INNER JOIN T052
ON KNVV~ZTERM = T052~ZTERM
FOR ALL ENTRIES IN LT_KNVP
WHERE KNVV~KUNNR = LT_KNVP-KUNN2 "支払先
AND KNVV~VKORG = P_VKORG
AND KNVV~VTWEG = P_VTWEG
AND KNVV~SPART = P_SPART.
*   入力された得意先の支払条件(締め日付)が一致するかどうかチェック
IF SY-SUBRC = 0.
SORT LT_T052.    "すべてを昇順ソート
*     期限->値が小さいほうを残し削除
DELETE ADJACENT DUPLICATES FROM LT_T052
COMPARING LIFNR ZTERM.
SORT LT_T052 BY ZTAGG.
*     期限の重複を削除
DELETE ADJACENT DUPLICATES FROM LT_T052
COMPARING ZTAGG.
DESCRIBE TABLE LT_T052 LINES LW_LINES.
*     締め日付が複数ある場合はエラー
IF LW_LINES > 1.
MESSAGE E999(YN01) WITH TEXT-053
SPACE
SPACE
SPACE.
ENDIF.
READ TABLE LT_T052 INTO LW_T052 INDEX 1.
*     入力された照合締日と仕入先の締日日付が一致するかどうかチェック
IF P_CZFBDT IS INITIAL.
CALL FUNCTION 'YK_ZFBDT_GET_BY_KNVV'
EXPORTING
I_CORD               = LW_T052-LIFNR
I_VKORG              = P_VKORG
I_VTWEG              = P_VTWEG
I_SPART              = P_SPART
I_DAY                = SY-DATUM
IMPORTING
E_ZFBDT              = LW_ZFBDT
E_ZFBDT_OLD          = LW_ZFBDT_OLD
EXCEPTIONS
NO_GET_T052          = 1
NO_GOOD_GETDAY       = 2
NO_GET_ZTERM         = 3
OTHERS               = 4.
*** 2012/03/07 MOD START ４***
*        P_CZFBDT = LW_ZFBDT.
P_CZFBDT = LW_ZFBDT_OLD.
LW_CHECK = LW_ZFBDT_OLD.
*** 2012/03/07 MOD END ４***
ELSE.
CALL FUNCTION 'YK_ZFBDT_GET_BY_KNVV'
EXPORTING
I_CORD               = LW_T052-LIFNR
I_VKORG              = P_VKORG
I_VTWEG              = P_VTWEG
I_SPART              = P_SPART

IMPORTING

EXCEPTIONS
NO_GET_T052          = 1
NO_GOOD_GETDAY       = 2
NO_GET_ZTERM         = 3
OTHERS               = 4.
*** 2012/03/07 INSERT START ４***
LW_CHECK = LW_ZFBDT.
*** 2012/03/07 INSERT END ４***
ENDIF.

IF SY-SUBRC = 0.
*** 2012/03/07 MOD START ４***
*        IF LW_ZFBDT <> P_CZFBDT.
IF LW_CHECK <> P_CZFBDT.
*** 2012/03/07 MOD END ４***
*** 2012/03/07 MOD START ５***
*          WRITE LW_ZFBDT TO LW_MESSAGE.
*          MESSAGE E999(YN01) WITH TEXT-054 LW_MESSAGE
*                                  TEXT-055 SPACE.
MESSAGE E913(YN01).
*** 2012/03/07 MOD END ５***
ELSE.
*         検収日/請求日が初期値の場合は初期値提案
IF P_LDAT11[] IS INITIAL.
P_LDAT11-SIGN   = 'I'.
P_LDAT11-OPTION = 'BT'.
* 2012/03/05 MOD START
* LOW値は提案不要
*            P_LDAT11-LOW    = LW_ZFBDT_OLD + 1.
CLEAR: P_LDAT11-LOW.
* 2012/03/05 MOD END
*** 2012/03/07 MOD START ４***
*            P_LDAT11-HIGH   = LW_ZFBDT.
P_LDAT11-HIGH   = LW_CHECK.
*** 2012/03/07 MOD END ４***
APPEND P_LDAT11.
ENDIF.
IF P_LDAT12[] IS INITIAL.
P_LDAT12-SIGN   = 'I'.
P_LDAT12-OPTION = 'BT'.
* 2012/03/05 MOD START
* LOW値は提案不要
*            P_LDAT12-LOW    = LW_ZFBDT_OLD + 1.
CLEAR: P_LDAT12-LOW.
* 2012/03/05 MOD END
*** 2012/03/07 MOD START ４***

P_LDAT12-HIGH   = LW_CHECK.
*** 2012/03/07 MOD END ４***
APPEND P_LDAT12.

ENDIF.
ENDIF.

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  GET_WERKS_NAME
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       プラント名取得
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
*      -->P_YNDVSON         プラント
*      <--P_YNDVSONNAME     プラント名
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM GET_WERKS_NAME USING    P_DVSON
CHANGING P_DVSONNAME.
DATA:LW_WERKS_NAME   TYPE TYP_WERKS_NAME.

CHECK NOT P_DVSON IS INITIAL.
* 内部テーブルを検索
READ TABLE T_WERKS_NAME INTO LW_WERKS_NAME
WITH TABLE KEY WERKS = P_DVSON.
* すでに取得している場合はこの値を取得
IF SY-SUBRC = 0.
P_DVSONNAME = LW_WERKS_NAME-NAME1.
ELSE.
*   まだ取得していない場合は、 ＤＢより取得
SELECT SINGLE
WERKS
NAME1
INTO LW_WERKS_NAME
FROM T001W
WHERE WERKS = P_DVSON.   "プラント
*   内部テーブルに格納しておく
INSERT LW_WERKS_NAME INTO TABLE T_WERKS_NAME.
P_DVSONNAME = LW_WERKS_NAME-NAME1.
ENDIF.

ENDFORM.                    " GET_WERKS_NAME
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  GET_YNPERNR_NAME
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       担当者名称取得
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
*      -->P_L_H_GRID_DATA_YNPERNR  text
*      <--P_L_H_GRID_DATA_YNPERNRNAME  text
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM GET_YNPERNR_NAME USING    P_PERNR
CHANGING P_PERNRNAME.
DATA:LW_PERNR_NAME   TYPE TYP_PERNR_NAME.

CHECK NOT P_PERNR IS INITIAL.
* 内部テーブルを検索
READ TABLE T_PERNR_NAME INTO LW_PERNR_NAME
WITH TABLE KEY PERNR = P_PERNR.
* すでに取得している場合はこの値を取得
IF SY-SUBRC = 0.
P_PERNRNAME = LW_PERNR_NAME-NAME_TEXT.
ELSE.
*   まだ取得していない場合は、 ＤＢより取得
SELECT BNAME
NAME_TEXT
INTO LW_PERNR_NAME
FROM USR21 INNER JOIN ADRP
ON USR21~PERSNUMBER = ADRP~PERSNUMBER
UP TO 1 ROWS
WHERE BNAME = P_PERNR+0(12).
ENDSELECT.
*   内部テーブルに格納しておく
INSERT LW_PERNR_NAME INTO TABLE T_PERNR_NAME.
P_PERNRNAME = LW_PERNR_NAME-NAME_TEXT.
ENDIF.

ENDFORM.                    " GET_YNPERNR_NAME
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  INSERT_DATA_INIT_LINE
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       外部データ登録時のデフォルト行編集
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
*      <--P_GRID_DATA_0200   外部データ入力ALV構造
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM INSERT_DATA_INIT_LINE CHANGING P_GRID_DATA_0200
TYPE TYP_GRID_DATA_0200.

*-- 会社コード
P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNBUKRS = G_BUKRS_INPUT.
*-- 担当者
P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNPERNR = SY-UNAME.
*-- 担当者名称
PERFORM GET_YNPERNR_NAME    USING P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNPERNR
CHANGING P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNPERNRNAME.
*-- 営業所/プラント
IF P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNDVSON IS INITIAL.
*   選択画面に入力されている営業所/プラントを取得
PERFORM INSERT_DATA_INT_DVSON CHANGING P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNDVSON.

* -- 営業所名/プラント名
IF P_MODE = C_MODE_SALES.        "売上の場合
IF P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNDVSON <> SPACE.
PERFORM GET_VKBUR_NAME USING P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNDVSON
P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNDVSONNAME.
ENDIF.
ENDIF.
IF P_MODE = C_MODE_PURCHASE.     "仕入の場合
IF P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNDVSON <> SPACE.
PERFORM GET_WERKS_NAME    USING P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNDVSON
CHANGING P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNDVSONNAME.
ENDIF.
ENDIF.

*-- 受注先/発注先
IF P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNLIST1 IS INITIAL.
*     選択画面に入力されている受注先/発注先を取得
PERFORM INSERT_DATA_INT_LIST1 CHANGING P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNLIST1.

*-- 受注先/発注先名
PERFORM GET_VRFCTON_NAME USING    P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNLIST1
CHANGING P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNLIST1NAME.
ENDIF.

ENDIF.

ENDFORM.                    " INSERT_DATA_INIT_LINE
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  INSERT_DATA_INT_DVSON
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       外部データ登録時の営業所/プラント初期値データ
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
*      <--P_YNDVSON          営業所/プラント
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM INSERT_DATA_INT_DVSON CHANGING P_YNDVSON.

FIELD-SYMBOLS: <FS1>, <FS2>, <FS3>.
DATA: LW_CNT   TYPE I.

LOOP AT P_DVSON1.
LW_CNT = LW_CNT + 1.
*   選択画面に入力された1件目のデータを取得
IF LW_CNT = 1.
ASSIGN COMPONENT 1 OF STRUCTURE P_DVSON1 TO <FS1>.
ASSIGN COMPONENT 2 OF STRUCTURE P_DVSON1 TO <FS2>.
IF <FS2> <> 'CP'.
ASSIGN COMPONENT 3 OF STRUCTURE P_DVSON1 TO <FS3>.
P_YNDVSON = <FS3>.
ENDIF.
*   プラント/営業所に複数入力がある場合は初期提案しない
ELSE.
CLEAR:P_YNDVSON.
ENDIF.
ENDLOOP.

ENDFORM.                    " INSERT_DATA_INT_DVSON
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  SET_T_GRID_DATA_0200_DEFAULT_M
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       外部データ登録時のデフォルト設定
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM SET_T_GRID_DATA_0200_DEFAULT_M.

FIELD-SYMBOLS: <FS> TYPE TYP_GRID_DATA_0200.
DATA:LW_TABIX     TYPE SY-TABIX,       " 現在の行番号
LW_SET_WAERS TYPE CHAR01,
LW_KNVP      TYPE TYP_KNVP_0200.

LOOP AT T_GRID_DATA_0200 ASSIGNING <FS>.
LW_TABIX = SY-TABIX.
CLEAR:LW_SET_WAERS.
*   売上/仕入デフォルト設定（最初の1回のみ）
IF <FS>-YNBUKRS IS INITIAL.
PERFORM INSERT_DATA_INIT_LINE CHANGING <FS>.
ENDIF.

*   売上入力項目連動のデフォルト設定（毎回処理）
IF P_MODE = C_MODE_SALES.        "売上の場合
PERFORM GET_DATA3_INIT_LINE    USING LW_TABIX
CHANGING <FS>
LW_SET_WAERS
LW_KNVP.
ENDIF.

*   仕入入力項目連動のデフォルト設定（毎回処理）
IF P_MODE = C_MODE_PURCHASE.     "仕入の場合
PERFORM GET_DATA2_INIT_LINE    USING LW_TABIX
CHANGING <FS>
LW_SET_WAERS.
ENDIF.
*   売上時金額計算
IF P_MODE = C_MODE_SALES.        "売上の場合
PERFORM CALC_DATA2_INIT_LINE    USING LW_SET_WAERS
LW_KNVP
CHANGING <FS>.
ENDIF.
*   仕入時金額計算
IF P_MODE = C_MODE_PURCHASE.     "仕入の場合
PERFORM CALC_DATA_INIT_LINE    USING LW_SET_WAERS
CHANGING <FS>.
ENDIF.
ENDLOOP.
*  CLEAR:T_CHANGE_CURRENT.
ENDFORM.                    " SET_T_GRID_DATA_0200_DEFAULT_M

LW_VRFCTON.

**-- 照合キー：1 発注伝票番号へコピー

*** 2012/07/12 INSERT START ***　登録時請求先初期値でマスタ値提案
*-- 登録かつ請求先初期値の場合、マスタ値提案
IF  INPUT_MODE = C_INPUT_MODE_NEW.
IF P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNVRFCTON IS INITIAL.
*-- 登録かつ請求先初期値でない場合、何もしない。
*** 2012/07/12 INSERT END ***
* 取引先機能データの取得
LW_LIFNR = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNLIST1+0(10).
CALL FUNCTION 'CONVERSION_EXIT_ALPHA_INPUT'
EXPORTING
INPUT         = LW_LIFNR
IMPORTING
OUTPUT        = LW_LIFNR.
CLEAR:LW_WYT3.
* 発注先に紐づく請求先を取得
READ TABLE T_WYT3 INTO LW_WYT3
WITH TABLE KEY LIFNR = LW_LIFNR
EKORG = P_EKORG.
IF SY-SUBRC = 0.
ELSE.
SELECT WYT3~LIFNR
WYT3~EKORG
WYT3~LIFN2
LFM1~WAERS
INTO LW_WYT3

ON  WYT3~LIFNR = LFM1~LIFNR

UP TO 1 ROWS

AND WYT3~EKORG = P_EKORG

*-- 請求先
P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNVRFCTON = LW_WYT3-LIFN2.
*** 2012/07/12 INSERT START ***　同上
ENDIF.
ENDIF.
*** 2012/07/12 INSERT END ***

*** 2012/07/12 INSERT STRAT ***　発注先に合わせた通貨コード提案
*-- 発注先に合わせた通貨コードの自動提案
IF P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNLIST1 IS INITIAL.
ELSE.
CLEAR LW_LIFNR.
LW_LIFNR = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNLIST1+0(10).
CALL FUNCTION 'CONVERSION_EXIT_ALPHA_INPUT'
EXPORTING
INPUT         = LW_LIFNR
IMPORTING

AND EKORG = P_EKORG.
ENDIF.

*-- 会計年度(毎回必ず更新)

*** 2012/07/12 DEL START ***　通貨提案削除
**-- 通貨コード
*  IF      P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNWAERS IS INITIAL
*  AND NOT LW_WYT3-WAERS            IS INITIAL.
*    P_SET_WAERS = C_ON.   "通貨コード設定フラグをON
*  ENDIF.
*  P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNWAERS = LW_WYT3-WAERS.
*** 2012/07/12 DEL END ***

*** 2012/03/26 INSERT START ２***
* 該当レコードの請求先の外部EXIT番号を取得する。
*** 2012/07/12 MOD START ***　EXIT番号の取得方法変更
*  READ TABLE T_YN230 INTO W_YN230
*       WITH KEY VRFCTON = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNVRFCTON
*                BUKRS   = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNBUKRS.
*-- 本時点で、請求先と発注先の紐付けは、崩れている可能性がある。
SELECT SINGLE OUTEXITDOC
INTO W_YN230-OUTEXITDOC
FROM YN230
WHERE VRFCTON = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNVRFCTON
AND BUKRS   = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNBUKRS.
*** 2012/07/12 MOD END ***
IF SY-SUBRC NE 0.
CONCATENATE 'D-' P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNWAERS
INTO LW_VRFCTON.
READ TABLE T_YN230 INTO W_YN230
WITH KEY VRFCTON = LW_VRFCTON
BUKRS   = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNBUKRS.
ENDIF.

IF     W_YN230-OUTEXITDOC = '2001'.
**-- 照合キー：1 発注伝票番号へコピー
P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNCKEY1 = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNLIST2+0(10).
CLEAR P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNCKEY2.

ELSEIF W_YN230-OUTEXITDOC = '2002'.
**-- 照合キー：2 インボイスNOへコピー
P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNCKEY2 = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNLIST8.
CLEAR P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNCKEY1.

ELSEIF W_YN230-OUTEXITDOC = '2003'.
**-- 照合キー：1 発注伝票番号へコピー
P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNCKEY1 = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNLIST2+0(10).
**-- 照合キー：2 インボイスNOへコピー
P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNCKEY2 = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNLIST8.

ENDIF.
*** 2012/03/26 INSERT END ２***

*-- 計上締日(未入力の場合のみ)
IF  NOT P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNLIST1  IS INITIAL   "受注先が設定
AND NOT P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNLDATE1 IS INITIAL.  "請求日が設定
LW_CORD = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNLIST1.
LW_DAY =  P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNLDATE1.
CALL FUNCTION 'YK_ZFBDT_GET_BY_LFM1'
EXPORTING
I_CORD               = LW_CORD
I_EKORG              = P_EKORG
I_DAY                = LW_DAY
I_ZTERM              = SPACE
IMPORTING
E_ZFBDT              = LW_ZFBDT
EXCEPTIONS
NO_GET_T052          = 1
NO_GOOD_GETDAY       = 2
NO_GET_ZTERM         = 3
OTHERS               = 4.
IF SY-SUBRC <> 0.
CLEAR:LW_ZFBDT.
ENDIF.
P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNZFBDT = LW_ZFBDT.
ENDIF.

ENDFORM.                    " GET_DATA2_INIT_LINE
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  CALC_DATA_INIT_LINE
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       [仕入]外部データ登録時の金額項目デフォルト値編集
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
*      -->P_SET_WAERS        税コード取得フラグ
*      <--P_GRID_DATA_0200   外部データ入力ALV構造
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM CALC_DATA_INIT_LINE    USING P_SET_WAERS TYPE CHAR01
CHANGING P_GRID_DATA_0200
TYPE TYP_GRID_DATA_0200.
DATA:LW_YNKNITXAMT TYPE YNITXAMT,        " 税抜金額(外部表記)
LW_WRBTR    TYPE WRBTR,             " 属性変換用
LT_MWDAT    TYPE TABLE OF RTAX1U15, " 税額
LW_MWDAT    LIKE LINE  OF LT_MWDAT,
LW_KNUMH    TYPE KNUMH,             " 条件レコード番号
LW_MWSKZ    TYPE TYP_MWSKZ.

*-- 通貨コードが入力されている場合のみ自動計算
CHECK NOT P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNWAERS IS INITIAL.

* 2012/04/18 ADD START
*-- 税抜きと消費税の両方が初期値のときのみ計算処理
IF  P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNKNITXAMT = 0
AND P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNKNTAXAMT = 0.
ELSE.
*-- 税込金額(必ず更新する)
P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNKNETXAMT = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNKNTAXAMT +
P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNKNITXAMT.
EXIT.
ENDIF.
* 2012/04/18 ADD END

*--税抜金額(数量×単価)(未入力の場合に設定)
IF  P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNKNITXAMT = 0.
LW_YNKNITXAMT = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNKNQUAN *
P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNKNUNTPRC.
*   金額の内部換算
PERFORM CURRENCY_INTERNAL    USING P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNWAERS
LW_YNKNITXAMT
CHANGING P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNKNITXAMT.
ENDIF.

*--消費税額(未入力の場合に設定)
IF  P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNKNTAXAMT = 0
AND P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNKNITXAMT <> 0.

LW_WRBTR = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNKNITXAMT.     "税抜金額(内部)
*** 2012/03/26 DEL START １***
**   税コードを取得
*    READ TABLE T_MWSKZ INTO LW_MWSKZ
*         WITH TABLE KEY LIFNR = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNLIST1+0(10).
*    IF SY-SUBRC <> 0.
*** 2012/03/26 DEL END １***
*     発注先をキーに条件マスタを検索
SELECT SINGLE KNUMH
INTO LW_KNUMH
FROM A044
WHERE KAPPL = P_KAPPL
AND KSCHL = P_KSCHL
AND EKORG = P_EKORG
AND LIFNR = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNLIST1+0(10)
*** 2012/03/26 MOD START １***
*         AND DATBI >= SY-DATUM
*         AND DATAB <= SY-DATUM.
AND DATBI >= P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNLDATE1
AND DATAB <= P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNLDATE1.
*** 2012/03/26 MOD END １***
IF  SY-SUBRC = 0.
SELECT KONP~MWSK1
INTO LW_MWSKZ-MWSKZ
FROM KONP
UP TO 1 ROWS
WHERE KNUMH = LW_KNUMH.
ENDSELECT.
IF SY-SUBRC = 0.
LW_MWSKZ-LIFNR = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNLIST1+0(10).
INSERT LW_MWSKZ INTO TABLE T_MWSKZ.
ENDIF.
ENDIF.
*** 2012/03/26 DEL START １***
*    ENDIF.
*** 2012/03/26 DEL END １***

*   税抜金額分の税額を税コードを使用して算出
IF LW_MWSKZ-MWSKZ IS INITIAL.
ELSE.
CALL FUNCTION 'CALCULATE_TAX_FROM_NET_AMOUNT'
EXPORTING
I_BUKRS           = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNBUKRS
I_MWSKZ           = LW_MWSKZ-MWSKZ
I_WAERS           = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNWAERS
I_WRBTR           = LW_WRBTR
TABLES
T_MWDAT           = LT_MWDAT
EXCEPTIONS
BUKRS_NOT_FOUND   = 1
COUNTRY_NOT_FOUND = 2
MWSKZ_NOT_DEFINED = 3
MWSKZ_NOT_VALID   = 4
KTOSL_NOT_FOUND   = 5
KALSM_NOT_FOUND   = 6
PARAMETER_ERROR   = 7
KNUMH_NOT_FOUND   = 8
KSCHL_NOT_FOUND   = 9
UNKNOWN_ERROR     = 10
ACCOUNT_NOT_FOUND = 11
TXJCD_NOT_VALID   = 12
OTHERS            = 13.
IF SY-SUBRC <> 0.
P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNKNTAXAMT = 0.
ENDIF.

READ TABLE LT_MWDAT INTO LW_MWDAT INDEX 1.
P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNKNTAXAMT = LW_MWDAT-WMWST.
ENDIF.

* 入力した際に通貨コード"JPY"にもかかわらず、内部テーブルの値が
* 円内部換算されないため、内部換算を行う↓↓↓
* 税額に入力がある場合
ELSE.
IF P_SET_WAERS = C_ON.      "今回通貨コードが設定された場合
LW_MWDAT-WMWST = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNKNTAXAMT.
PERFORM CURRENCY_INTERNAL    USING P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNWAERS
LW_MWDAT-WMWST
CHANGING P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNKNTAXAMT.
ENDIF.
ENDIF.

* 税抜き金額が入力があり、今回通貨コードが設定された場合
IF  P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNKNITXAMT <> 0
AND P_SET_WAERS = C_ON.
LW_MWDAT-WMWST = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNKNITXAMT.
PERFORM CURRENCY_INTERNAL    USING P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNWAERS
LW_MWDAT-WMWST
CHANGING P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNKNITXAMT.
ENDIF.
"ここまで↑↑

*-- 税込金額(必ず更新する)
P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNKNETXAMT = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNKNTAXAMT +
P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNKNITXAMT.

ENDFORM.                    " CALC_DATA_INIT_LINE
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  CURRENCY_INTERNAL
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       金額項目の内部換算
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
*      -->P_YNWAERS         通貨コード
*      -->P_IN              換算元金額
*      <--P_OUT             換算後金額
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM CURRENCY_INTERNAL USING    P_YNWAERS
P_IN
CHANGING P_OUT.
DATA:LW_BAPICURR TYPE BAPICURR_D,        " 消費税額
LW_CURRENCY TYPE WAERS_CURC,        " 通貨コード
LW_RETURN   TYPE BAPIRETURN.        " リターン

LW_BAPICURR = P_IN.
LW_CURRENCY = P_YNWAERS.      "通貨コード

CALL FUNCTION 'BAPI_CURRENCY_CONV_TO_INTERNAL'
EXPORTING
CURRENCY             = LW_CURRENCY
AMOUNT_EXTERNAL      = LW_BAPICURR
MAX_NUMBER_OF_DIGITS = '20'
IMPORTING
AMOUNT_INTERNAL      = P_OUT
RETURN               = LW_RETURN.

ENDFORM.                    " CURRENCY_INTERNAL
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  CHECK_VRFCTON_IN
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       外部データ入力[仕入先]選択画面の値かどうかチェック
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
*      -->P_LH_GRID_DATA_YNVRFCTON  text
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM CHECK_VRFCTON_IN USING    P_VRFCTON.

CLEAR:RC_CODE.
* 自社データの受注先(外部データの受注先も同じ値)と条件が一致するかどうか
IF P_VRFCTON IN P_LIST12.
"正常
ELSE.
RC_CODE = C_RC_CODE_ERROR.
ENDIF.

ENDFORM.                    " CHECK_VRFCTON_IN
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  GET_YN130
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       売上照合マスタよりデータ取得
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM GET_YN130.
DATA:LT_YN130   TYPE STANDARD TABLE OF TYP_YN130.

CLEAR:T_YN130.

* 自社データ分
SELECT KNVP~KUNNR
YN130~VRFCTON
YN130~BUKRS
YN130~WAERS
YN130~OUTEXITDOC
INTO TABLE T_YN130
FROM KNVP INNER JOIN YN130
ON KNVP~KUNN2 = YN130~VRFCTON
WHERE KNVP~KUNNR IN P_LIST12         "受注先
AND KNVP~VKORG  = P_VKORG
AND KNVP~VTWEG  = P_VTWEG
AND KNVP~SPART  = P_SPART
AND KNVP~PARVW  = P_PARVWK
*** 2012/03/07 MOD START ６***
*     AND KNVP~PARZA  = SPACE
AND KNVP~PARZA  = '000'
*** 2012/03/07 MOD END ６***
AND YN130~BUKRS = G_BUKRS_INPUT.

* 選択画面の受注先紐付く支払人のEXIT番号を取得した後
* デフォルトデータを取得
SELECT VRFCTON
BUKRS
WAERS
OUTEXITDOC
INTO CORRESPONDING FIELDS OF TABLE LT_YN130
FROM YN130
WHERE VRFCTON LIKE 'D-%'
AND BUKRS = G_BUKRS_INPUT.
APPEND LINES OF LT_YN130 TO T_YN130.

SORT T_YN130.
ENDFORM.                    " GET_YN130
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  GET_YN230
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       仕入照合マスタよりデータ取得
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM GET_YN230.
*** 2012/03/07 INSERT START ６***
DATA:LT_YN230   TYPE STANDARD TABLE OF TYP_YN230.
*** 2012/03/07 INSERT END ６***
*** 2012/03/07 DEL START ６***
*  CLEAR:T_YN130.
*** 2012/03/07 DEL END ６***
* 選択画面の仕入先に'D-*'を追加しデータ取得

CLEAR:T_YN230.

* 自社データ分
SELECT WYT3~LIFNR
YN230~VRFCTON
YN230~BUKRS
YN230~WAERS
YN230~OUTEXITDOC
INTO TABLE T_YN230
FROM WYT3 INNER JOIN YN230
ON WYT3~LIFN2 = YN230~VRFCTON
WHERE WYT3~LIFNR IN P_LIST11         "発注先
AND WYT3~EKORG  = P_EKORG
*** 2012/03/07 INSERT START ６***
AND WYT3~LTSNR  = SPACE
AND WYT3~WERKS  = SPACE
*** 2012/03/07 INSERT END ６***
AND WYT3~PARVW  = P_PARVW          "請求先
*** 2012/03/07 INSERT START ６***
AND WYT3~PARZA  = '000'
*** 2012/03/07 INSERT END ６***
AND YN230~BUKRS = G_BUKRS_INPUT.
*** 2012/03/07 INSERT START ６***
* 選択画面の発注先に紐付く請求先のEXIT番号を取得した後
* デフォルトデータを取得
SELECT VRFCTON
BUKRS
WAERS
OUTEXITDOC
INTO CORRESPONDING FIELDS OF TABLE LT_YN230
FROM YN230
WHERE VRFCTON LIKE 'D-%'
AND BUKRS = G_BUKRS_INPUT.
APPEND LINES OF LT_YN230 TO T_YN230.
*** 2012/03/07 INSERT END ６***
*** 2012/03/07 DEL START ６***
*  IF SY-SUBRC = 0.
*** 2012/03/07 DEL END ６***
SORT T_YN230.
*** 2012/03/07 DEL START ６***
*  ENDIF.
*** 2012/03/07 DEL END ６***

ENDFORM.                    " GET_YN230
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  LIST1_CHECK_TYPE
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       得意先/仕入先の必須項目を決定するEXIT番号取得
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
*      -->P_YNLIST1          受注先/発注先
*      -->P_YNWAERS          通貨コード
*      <--P_EXIT_TYPE        EXIT番号
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM LIST1_CHECK_TYPE USING    P_YNLIST1     TYPE ANY
P_YNWAERS     TYPE ANY
CHANGING P_EXIT_TYPE   TYPE YNOUTEXITDOC.
DATA:L_LIFNR    TYPE LIFNR,
L_YN230    TYPE TYP_YN230,
L_YN130    TYPE TYP_YN130,
LW_WAERS   TYPE WAERS.        "通貨コード取得用

CLEAR:P_EXIT_TYPE.
CALL FUNCTION 'CONVERSION_EXIT_ALPHA_INPUT'
EXPORTING
INPUT         = P_YNLIST1
IMPORTING
OUTPUT        = L_LIFNR.

IF P_MODE = C_MODE_SALES.        "売上の場合
*   処理の最初に取得していた仕入照合マスタを読み込む
READ TABLE T_YN130 INTO L_YN130
WITH KEY KUNNR = L_LIFNR        "受注先
BUKRS = G_BUKRS_INPUT
BINARY SEARCH.
*   受注先で読み込めない場合は通貨コードのデフォルト値で検索
IF SY-SUBRC <> 0.
IF P_YNWAERS <> SPACE.
CONCATENATE 'D-' P_YNWAERS
INTO G_X30_DEFAULT.
ELSE.
*       支払人の通貨コードを取得
SELECT SINGLE KNVV~WAERS
INTO LW_WAERS
FROM KNVP INNER JOIN KNVV
ON  KNVP~KUNN2 = KNVV~KUNNR
AND KNVP~VKORG = KNVV~VKORG
AND KNVP~VTWEG = KNVV~VTWEG
AND KNVP~SPART = KNVV~SPART
WHERE KNVP~KUNNR = L_LIFNR
AND KNVP~VKORG = P_VKORG
AND KNVP~VTWEG = P_VTWEG
AND KNVP~SPART = P_SPART
AND KNVP~PARVW = P_PARVWK
AND KNVP~PARZA = SPACE.
IF SY-SUBRC = 0.
CONCATENATE 'D-' LW_WAERS
INTO G_X30_DEFAULT.
ELSE.
CLEAR:G_X30_DEFAULT.
ENDIF.
ENDIF.
*     デフォルト値で読み込み
READ TABLE T_YN130 INTO L_YN130
WITH KEY VRFCTON = G_X30_DEFAULT
BUKRS = G_BUKRS_INPUT.
ENDIF.
P_EXIT_TYPE = L_YN130-OUTEXITDOC.
ENDIF.

IF P_MODE = C_MODE_PURCHASE.     "仕入の場合
*   処理の最初に取得していた仕入照合マスタを読み込む
READ TABLE T_YN230 INTO L_YN230
WITH KEY LIFNR = L_LIFNR        "発注先
BUKRS = G_BUKRS_INPUT
BINARY SEARCH.
*   発注先で読み込めない場合は通貨コードのデフォルト値で検索
IF SY-SUBRC <> 0.
IF P_YNWAERS <> SPACE.
CONCATENATE 'D-' P_YNWAERS
INTO G_X30_DEFAULT.
ELSE.
*       請求先の通貨コードを取得
SELECT SINGLE LFM1~WAERS
INTO LW_WAERS
FROM WYT3 INNER JOIN LFM1
ON  WYT3~LIFN2 = LFM1~LIFNR
AND WYT3~EKORG = LFM1~EKORG
WHERE WYT3~LIFNR = L_LIFNR
AND WYT3~EKORG = P_EKORG
AND WYT3~PARVW = P_PARVW.
IF SY-SUBRC = 0.
CONCATENATE 'D-' LW_WAERS
INTO G_X30_DEFAULT.
ELSE.
CLEAR:G_X30_DEFAULT.
ENDIF.
ENDIF.
*     デフォルト値で読み込み
READ TABLE T_YN230 INTO L_YN230
WITH KEY VRFCTON = G_X30_DEFAULT
BUKRS = G_BUKRS_INPUT.
ENDIF.
P_EXIT_TYPE = L_YN230-OUTEXITDOC.
ENDIF.

ENDFORM.                    " LIST1_CHECK_TYPE
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  CHANGE_ZYUTYU
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       選択画面受注先前ゼロ埋め
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
*FORM CHANGE_ZYUTYU.
*
*  DATA: L_CHAR10(10) TYPE C,
*        LW_LIST1  LIKE LINE OF GR_LIFNR,
*        LW_LIST12 LIKE LINE OF P_LIST12.
*
** 選択画面に入力された受注先の前ゼロ埋め
*  CLEAR:GR_LIFNR.
*  LOOP AT P_LIST12 INTO LW_LIST12.
*    LW_LIST1 = LW_LIST12.
*    L_CHAR10 = LW_LIST12-LOW+0(10).
*    CALL FUNCTION 'CONVERSION_EXIT_ALPHA_INPUT'
*      EXPORTING
*        INPUT         = L_CHAR10
*      IMPORTING
*        OUTPUT        = L_CHAR10.
*    LW_LIST1-LOW = L_CHAR10.
*    APPEND LW_LIST1 TO GR_LIFNR.
*  ENDLOOP.
*
*ENDFORM.                    " CHANGE_ZYUTYU
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  INSERT_POINT_COMPARA_DATA
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       部分照合データの作成
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM INSERT_POINT_COMPARA_DATA.

DATA:LS_COMPARE TYPE TYP_COMPARE2,
LS_GRID_DATA TYPE TYP_GRID_DATA_0100,
LW_KNETXAMT  TYPE YNETXAMT,
LW_MESSAGE   TYPE SYMSGV,
LW_COMP      TYPE TYP_COMPARE,
LT_COMPARE   TYPE STANDARD TABLE OF TYP_COMPARE2,
LW_TABLE     TYPE CHAR10,
LW_RATE_FLG  TYPE CHAR1,             "換算レート設定フラグ
LW_KURSF     TYPE KURSF,             "換算レート
LW_ZUONR     TYPE DZUONR,            "ソートキー
LW_ZTERM     TYPE DZTERM.            "支払条件

* 作成した自社データ格納内部テーブル
DATA:LT_UPDATE         TYPE STANDARD TABLE OF TYP_GRID_DATA_0100.

CLEAR:RC_CODE, GT_POINT_COMPARE.

* COMPARE外部データに区分を設定し１つの内部テーブルに編集
* 外部データ
LOOP AT T_COMPARE_1 INTO LW_COMP
WHERE YNCSTS = C_CSTS_OK.                "チェックokのもの
IF LW_COMP-POINT_COMPARE <> SPACE.       "部分照合データのみ
MOVE-CORRESPONDING LW_COMP TO LS_COMPARE.
LS_COMPARE-YNKUBUN = C_KUBUN_EXTERNAL. "区分設定
APPEND LS_COMPARE TO LT_COMPARE.
ENDIF.
ENDLOOP.
* 自社データ
LOOP AT T_COMPARE_2 INTO LW_COMP
WHERE YNCSTS = C_CSTS_OK.                "チェックokのもの
IF LW_COMP-POINT_COMPARE <> SPACE.        "部分照合データのみ
MOVE-CORRESPONDING LW_COMP TO LS_COMPARE.
LS_COMPARE-YNKUBUN = C_KUBUN_INTERNAL. "区分設定
APPEND LS_COMPARE TO LT_COMPARE.
ENDIF.
ENDLOOP.

* 部分照合データをループ
LOOP AT LT_COMPARE INTO LS_COMPARE.

*   今回照合したデータのうち、部分照合差額が入力されているものが処理対象
LOOP AT T_GRID_DATA_0100 INTO LS_GRID_DATA
WHERE YNKUBUN     = LS_COMPARE-YNKUBUN
AND YNBUKRS     = LS_COMPARE-YNBUKRS
AND YNVRFCTON   = LS_COMPARE-YNVRFCTON
AND YNTGTFLG    = C_ON
AND YNDELFLG    = C_OFF
AND YNCSTS      <> C_CSTS_OK_MANUAL
AND YNCSTS      <> C_CSTS_OK_AUTO
AND YNKNETXAMT4 <> 0.

CLEAR:LW_RATE_FLG, LW_KURSF, LW_ZUONR, LW_ZTERM.
*----- BDC用データ編集
PERFORM MAKE_POINT_DATA       USING LS_GRID_DATA
CHANGING LW_RATE_FLG  "換算レートフラグ
LW_KURSF     "換算レート
LW_ZUONR     "ソートキー
LW_ZTERM.    "支払条件
*----- 会計伝票作成
PERFORM MAKE_POINT_COMPARA_DOC     USING LW_RATE_FLG
LW_KURSF
LW_ZUONR
LW_ZTERM
CHANGING LS_GRID_DATA
RC_CODE.
IF RC_CODE <> 0.
ROLLBACK WORK.
MESSAGE I909.
EXIT.
ENDIF.

*----- ＤＢデータ作成
LW_KNETXAMT = LS_GRID_DATA-YNKNETXAMT4.
LS_GRID_DATA-YNCHKDOC = LS_COMPARE-YNCHKDOC.
LS_GRID_DATA-YNCHKDAT = LS_COMPARE-YNCHKDAT.
LS_GRID_DATA-YNCHKUSR = LS_COMPARE-YNCHKUSR.
APPEND LS_GRID_DATA TO LT_UPDATE.
ENDLOOP.

*   ＢＤＣエラーが発生している場合は処理を終了
IF RC_CODE <> 0.
EXIT.
ENDIF.
ENDLOOP.

*----- すべてのＢＤＣが正常に終了した後にYN120,YN220にデータ作成
CHECK RC_CODE IS INITIAL.
*----- 更新ＤＢ設定(エラーメッセージ用)
CASE P_MODE.
*  【売上照合】
WHEN C_MODE_SALES.
LW_TABLE = 'YN120'.
*   【仕入照合】
WHEN C_MODE_PURCHASE.
LW_TABLE = 'YN220'.
WHEN OTHERS.
ENDCASE.

*----- 更新データをループし、ＤＢに反映
LOOP AT LT_UPDATE INTO LS_GRID_DATA.
IF LS_GRID_DATA-YNKNETXAMT4 < 0.
LW_KNETXAMT = LS_GRID_DATA-YNKNETXAMT4  * -1.
ELSE.
LW_KNETXAMT = LS_GRID_DATA-YNKNETXAMT4.
ENDIF.

*   外部データにプラスの金額を部分照合差額に入力した場合
IF  LS_GRID_DATA-YNKUBUN = C_KUBUN_EXTERNAL
AND LS_GRID_DATA-YNKNETXAMT4 > 0.
PERFORM INSERT_YN_20_POINT_COMPARA USING LS_GRID_DATA
C_CSTS_INIT
C_CSTS_OK
C_KUBUN_EXTERNAL
LW_KNETXAMT
CHANGING RC_CODE.

*   外部データにマイナスの金額を部分照合差額に入力した場合
ELSEIF LS_GRID_DATA-YNKUBUN = C_KUBUN_EXTERNAL
AND LS_GRID_DATA-YNKNETXAMT4 < 0.
PERFORM INSERT_YN_20_POINT_COMPARA USING LS_GRID_DATA
C_CSTS_OK
C_CSTS_INIT
C_KUBUN_EXTERNAL
LW_KNETXAMT
CHANGING RC_CODE.

*   自社データにプラスの金額を部分照合差額に入力した場合
ELSEIF LS_GRID_DATA-YNKUBUN = C_KUBUN_INTERNAL
AND LS_GRID_DATA-YNKNETXAMT4 > 0.
PERFORM INSERT_YN_20_POINT_COMPARA USING LS_GRID_DATA
C_CSTS_INIT
C_CSTS_OK
C_KUBUN_INTERNAL
LW_KNETXAMT
CHANGING RC_CODE.

*   自社データにマイナスの金額を部分照合差額に入力した場合
ELSEIF LS_GRID_DATA-YNKUBUN = C_KUBUN_INTERNAL
AND LS_GRID_DATA-YNKNETXAMT4 < 0.
PERFORM INSERT_YN_20_POINT_COMPARA USING LS_GRID_DATA
C_CSTS_OK
C_CSTS_INIT
C_KUBUN_INTERNAL
LW_KNETXAMT
CHANGING RC_CODE.

ENDIF.

IF RC_CODE <> 0.
ROLLBACK WORK.
MESSAGE I910 WITH LW_TABLE.
EXIT.
ENDIF.
ENDLOOP.

ENDFORM.                    " INSERT_POINT_COMPARA_DATA
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  MAKE_POINT_COMPARA_DOC
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       部分照合データ/会計伝票登録
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
*      -->P_RATE_FLG        換算レート設定フラグ
*      -->P_KURSF           換算レート
*      -->P_ZUONR           ソートキー
*      -->P_ZTERM           支払条件
*      <--P_GRID_DATA       部分照合差額が入力されたデータ
*      <--P_RC_CODE         リターンコード(エラーハンドリング用)
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM MAKE_POINT_COMPARA_DOC    USING P_RATE_FLG  TYPE CHAR1
P_KURSF     TYPE KURSF
P_ZUONR     TYPE DZUONR
P_ZTERM     TYPE DZTERM
CHANGING P_GRID_DATA TYPE TYP_GRID_DATA_0100
P_RC_CODE   TYPE SY-SUBRC.

DATA:LT_BDC      TYPE STANDARD TABLE OF BDCDATA,
LW_FVAL     TYPE BDC_FVAL,
LW_OPT      TYPE CTU_PARAMS,
LT_MESSAGE  TYPE STANDARD TABLE OF BDCMSGCOLL,
LW_MESSAGE  TYPE BDCMSGCOLL,
LW_SCREEN   TYPE CHAR4.

* 売上/仕入のＢＤＣの違いは画面番号のみ
IF P_MODE = C_MODE_SALES.   "売上
LW_SCREEN = '0301'.
ELSE.                       "仕入
LW_SCREEN = '0302'.
ENDIF.

PERFORM BDC_DYNPRO    USING 'SAPMF05A'
'0100'
CHANGING LT_BDC.
PERFORM BDC_VALUE     USING 'BDC_OKCODE'             "Enter
'/00'
CHANGING LT_BDC.
PERFORM BDC_VALUE     USING 'BKPF-BLDAT'             "伝票日付
SY-DATUM
CHANGING LT_BDC.
PERFORM BDC_VALUE     USING 'BKPF-BLART'             "伝票タイプ
P_BLART
CHANGING LT_BDC.
PERFORM BDC_VALUE     USING 'BKPF-BUKRS'             "会社コード
P_GRID_DATA-YNBUKRS
CHANGING LT_BDC.
PERFORM BDC_VALUE     USING 'BKPF-BUDAT'             "転記日付
SY-DATUM
CHANGING LT_BDC.
PERFORM BDC_VALUE     USING 'BKPF-WAERS'             "通貨コード
P_GRID_DATA-YNWAERS
CHANGING LT_BDC.
IF P_RATE_FLG = C_ON.
LW_FVAL = P_KURSF.
CONDENSE LW_FVAL NO-GAPS.             "SPACEを削除
PERFORM BDC_VALUE     USING 'BKPF-KURSF'           "換算レート
LW_FVAL
CHANGING LT_BDC.
CLEAR:LW_FVAL.
ENDIF.

PERFORM BDC_VALUE     USING 'RF05A-NEWBS'            "転記キー
P_BSCHLS
CHANGING LT_BDC.
PERFORM BDC_VALUE     USING 'RF05A-NEWKO'            "勘定コード
P_GRID_DATA-YNVRFCTON    "請求先
CHANGING LT_BDC.
* ２画面目
PERFORM BDC_DYNPRO    USING 'SAPMF05A'
LW_SCREEN
CHANGING LT_BDC.
PERFORM BDC_VALUE     USING 'BDC_OKCODE'             "Enter
'/00'
CHANGING LT_BDC.
"金額を外部表記に編集
WRITE P_GRID_DATA-YNKNETXAMT4 TO LW_FVAL
CURRENCY P_GRID_DATA-YNWAERS.
TRANSLATE LW_FVAL USING '- , '.      "符号とカンマをSPACEに変換
CONDENSE LW_FVAL NO-GAPS.             "SPACEを削除
PERFORM BDC_VALUE     USING 'BSEG-WRBTR'             "金額
LW_FVAL
CHANGING LT_BDC.
PERFORM BDC_VALUE     USING 'RF05A-NEWBS'            "転記キー
P_BSCHLH
CHANGING LT_BDC.
PERFORM BDC_VALUE     USING 'RF05A-NEWKO'            "勘定コード
P_GRID_DATA-YNVRFCTON    "請求先
CHANGING LT_BDC.
IF P_GRID_DATA-YNKUBUN = C_KUBUN_INTERNAL.           "自社の場合
PERFORM BDC_VALUE     USING 'BSEG-ZUONR'           "ソートキー
P_ZUONR
CHANGING LT_BDC.
*** 2012/03/10 INSERT START ７***
ENDIF.
*** 2012/03/10 INSERT END ７***
PERFORM BDC_VALUE     USING 'BSEG-ZTERM'           "支払条件
P_ZTERM
CHANGING LT_BDC.
*** 2012/03/10 DEL START ７***
*  ENDIF.
*** 2012/03/10 DEL END ７***

* ３画面目
PERFORM BDC_DYNPRO    USING 'SAPMF05A'
LW_SCREEN
CHANGING LT_BDC.
PERFORM BDC_VALUE     USING 'BDC_OKCODE'
'=AB'                    "戻る
CHANGING LT_BDC.
PERFORM BDC_VALUE     USING 'BSEG-WRBTR'             "金額
LW_FVAL
CHANGING LT_BDC.
IF P_GRID_DATA-YNKUBUN = C_KUBUN_INTERNAL.           "自社の場合
PERFORM BDC_VALUE     USING 'BSEG-ZUONR'           "ソートキー
P_ZUONR
CHANGING LT_BDC.
*** 2012/03/10 INSERT START ７***
ENDIF.
*** 2012/03/10 INSERT END ７***
PERFORM BDC_VALUE     USING 'BSEG-ZTERM'           "支払条件
P_ZTERM
CHANGING LT_BDC.
*** 2012/03/10 DEL START ７***
*  ENDIF.
*** 2012/03/10 DEL END ７***

* ヘッダ画面
PERFORM BDC_DYNPRO    USING 'SAPMF05A'
'0700'
CHANGING LT_BDC.
PERFORM BDC_VALUE     USING 'BDC_OKCODE'             "保存
'=BU'
CHANGING LT_BDC.

LW_OPT-DISMODE = 'N'.
LW_OPT-UPDMODE = 'S'.
* ＢＤＣトランザクション実行
CALL TRANSACTION 'F-42'  USING LT_BDC
OPTIONS FROM LW_OPT
MESSAGES INTO LT_MESSAGE.
* 登録時のメッセージを検索
READ TABLE LT_MESSAGE INTO LW_MESSAGE
WITH KEY MSGTYP = 'S'
MSGID  = 'F5'
MSGNR  = '312'.

* 存在する場合は、会計伝票番号を取得
IF SY-SUBRC = 0.
P_GRID_DATA-YNBELNR = LW_MESSAGE-MSGV1.
ELSE.
P_RC_CODE =  C_RC_CODE_ERROR.
ENDIF.

ENDFORM.                    " MAKE_POINT_COMPARA_DOC
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  BDC_DYNPRO
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       BDCデータ作成
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
*      -->P_PROGRAM    BDC モジュールプール・プログラム
*      -->P_DYNPRO     BDC Dynpro 番号
*      <--P_T_BDC      BDC内部テーブル
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM BDC_DYNPRO USING   P_PROGRAM  TYPE ANY
P_DYNPRO   TYPE ANY
CHANGING P_T_BDC    TYPE TYP_BDCDATA.

DATA: LW_BDC TYPE BDCDATA.

LW_BDC-PROGRAM = P_PROGRAM.
LW_BDC-DYNPRO  = P_DYNPRO.
LW_BDC-DYNBEGIN = C_ON.
APPEND LW_BDC TO P_T_BDC.

ENDFORM.                    " BDC_DYNPRO
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  BDC_VALUE
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       BDCデータ作成
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
*      -->P_FNAME      項目名
*      -->P_FVAL       BDC 項目値
*      <--P_T_BDC      BDC内部テーブル
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM BDC_VALUE USING    P_FNAM  TYPE ANY
P_FVAL  TYPE ANY
CHANGING P_T_BDC  TYPE TYP_BDCDATA.
DATA: LW_BDC TYPE BDCDATA.

LW_BDC-FNAM = P_FNAM.
LW_BDC-FVAL  = P_FVAL.
APPEND LW_BDC TO P_T_BDC.

ENDFORM.                    " BDC_VALUE
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  INSERT_YN_20_POINT_COMPARA
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       データ登録
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
*      -->P_GRID_DATA         元データ
*      -->P_CSTS_1            明細１のステータス
*      -->P_CSTS_2            明細２のステータス
*      -->P_KUBUN             処理区分(10:外部,20:自社)
*      -->P_KNETXAMT          税込金額(部分照合差額)
*      <--P_RC_CODE           リターンコード(エラーハンドリング用)
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM INSERT_YN_20_POINT_COMPARA USING    P_GRID_DATA
TYPE TYP_GRID_DATA_0100
P_CSTS_1
P_CSTS_2
P_KUBUN
P_KNETXAMT
CHANGING P_RC_CODE.
DATA: L_TNAME(10)         TYPE C.
DATA: L_S_YN_20           LIKE YN120,
LW_GRID_DATA_0100   TYPE TYP_GRID_DATA_0100,
LW_KNETXAMT         TYPE YNETXAMT,
LW_YEAR             TYPE GJAHR,             "会計年度算出用
LW_POINT_COMPARE    TYPE TYP_POINT_COMPARE, "画面出力用データ
LW_GJAHR            TYPE YNDOCGJAHR,        "伝票会計年度
LW_SLPDOC           TYPE YNSLPDOC,          "伝票番号
LW_DTLDOC           TYPE YNDTLDOC.          "伝票明細番号
* 2012/04/11 ADD START
TYPES:BEGIN OF L_TYP_DTL,
DTLDOC TYPE YNDTLDOC,          "伝票明細番号
END OF L_TYP_DTL.
DATA:L_T_DTL TYPE SORTED TABLE OF L_TYP_DTL
WITH UNIQUE KEY DTLDOC,
L_W_DTL TYPE L_TYP_DTL.

REFRESH:L_T_DTL.
CLEAR:L_W_DTL.
* 2012/04/11 ADD END
CLEAR RC_CODE.

*----- 処理対象のＤＢ名称編集
CONCATENATE 'YN' P_MODE C_KUBUN_INTERNAL INTO L_TNAME.
*----- 会計年度算出
CALL FUNCTION 'BAPI_COMPANYCODE_GET_PERIOD'
EXPORTING
COMPANYCODEID = P_GRID_DATA-YNBUKRS
*** 2012/04/16 MOD START ***
*          POSTING_DATE  = P_GRID_DATA-YNLDATE1   "請求日/入庫日
POSTING_DATE  = SY-DATUM             "会計伝票転記日
*** 2012/04/16 MOD END ***
IMPORTING
FISCAL_YEAR   = LW_YEAR.

IF P_KUBUN = C_KUBUN_EXTERNAL.               "外部データの場合
LW_GJAHR    = P_GRID_DATA-YNGJAHR1.
LW_SLPDOC   = P_GRID_DATA-YNSLPDOC1.
* 2012/04/11 DEL START
*    LW_DTLDOC   = P_GRID_DATA-YNDTLDOC1 + 10000.
* 2012/04/11 DEL END
ELSE.                                        "自社データの場合
LW_GJAHR    = P_GRID_DATA-YNGJAHR2.
LW_SLPDOC   = P_GRID_DATA-YNSLPDOC2.
LW_DTLDOC   = P_GRID_DATA-YNDTLDOC2 + 10000.
ENDIF.

*----- 明細番号存在チェック
* 部分照合データが存在するかどうかチェック
* 存在する場合は最大値を取得する
* 2012/04/11 ADD START
IF  P_KUBUN = C_KUBUN_EXTERNAL.               "外部データの場合
SELECT DTLDOC
INTO TABLE L_T_DTL
FROM (L_TNAME)
WHERE GJAHR   = LW_GJAHR
AND SLPDOC  = LW_SLPDOC
AND DTLDOC  > 10000
AND VRFCTON = P_GRID_DATA-YNVRFCTON
AND BUKRS   = P_GRID_DATA-YNBUKRS.
CLEAR:LW_DTLDOC.
LOOP AT  L_T_DTL INTO L_W_DTL.
IF L_W_DTL-DTLDOC+2(4) = P_GRID_DATA-YNDTLDOC1+2(4).
LW_DTLDOC = L_W_DTL-DTLDOC.
ENDIF.
ENDLOOP.

IF LW_DTLDOC IS INITIAL.
LW_DTLDOC   = P_GRID_DATA-YNDTLDOC1 + 10000.
ELSE.
LW_DTLDOC   = LW_DTLDOC + 10000.
ENDIF.
ELSE.
* 2012/04/11 ADD END
** 2012/05/10 MOD START
*    SELECT DTLDOC
*      INTO LW_DTLDOC
*      FROM (L_TNAME)
*     WHERE GJAHR   = LW_GJAHR
*       AND SLPDOC  = LW_SLPDOC
*       AND DTLDOC  > 10000
*       AND VRFCTON = P_GRID_DATA-YNVRFCTON
*       AND BUKRS   = P_GRID_DATA-YNBUKRS.
*    ENDSELECT.
** 2012/04/11 ADD START
*    IF SY-SUBRC <> 0.
*      LW_DTLDOC = P_GRID_DATA-YNDTLDOC2 + 10000.
*    ELSE.
*      LW_DTLDOC = LW_DTLDOC + 10000.
*    ENDIF.
*  ENDIF.
** 2012/04/11 ADD END
*-- 外部データと同様、伝票/明細で既存明細番号をチェック
SELECT DTLDOC
INTO TABLE L_T_DTL
FROM (L_TNAME)
WHERE GJAHR   = LW_GJAHR
AND SLPDOC  = LW_SLPDOC
AND DTLDOC  > 10000
AND VRFCTON = P_GRID_DATA-YNVRFCTON
AND BUKRS   = P_GRID_DATA-YNBUKRS.
CLEAR:LW_DTLDOC.
LOOP AT  L_T_DTL INTO L_W_DTL.
IF L_W_DTL-DTLDOC+2(4) = P_GRID_DATA-YNDTLDOC2+2(4).
LW_DTLDOC = L_W_DTL-DTLDOC.
ENDIF.
ENDLOOP.

IF LW_DTLDOC IS INITIAL.
LW_DTLDOC   = P_GRID_DATA-YNDTLDOC2 + 10000.
ELSE.
LW_DTLDOC   = LW_DTLDOC + 10000.
ENDIF.
ENDIF.
* 2012/05/10 MOD END
* 2012/04/11 DEL START
** 取得できない場合
*  IF SY-SUBRC <> 0.
*    IF P_KUBUN = C_KUBUN_EXTERNAL.
*      LW_DTLDOC = P_GRID_DATA-YNDTLDOC1 + 10000.
*    ELSE.
*      LW_DTLDOC = P_GRID_DATA-YNDTLDOC2 + 10000.
*    ENDIF.
*  ELSE.
*    LW_DTLDOC = LW_DTLDOC + 10000.
*  ENDIF.
* 2012/04/11 DEL END

*-----１明細目
* DBデータ作成
L_S_YN_20-MANDT    = SY-MANDT.
L_S_YN_20-GJAHR    = LW_GJAHR.
L_S_YN_20-SLPDOC   = LW_SLPDOC.
L_S_YN_20-DTLDOC   = LW_DTLDOC.
L_S_YN_20-VRFCTON  = P_GRID_DATA-YNVRFCTON.
L_S_YN_20-BUKRS    = P_GRID_DATA-YNBUKRS.
L_S_YN_20-ZFBDT    = P_GRID_DATA-YNZFBDT.
L_S_YN_20-PRCTR    = P_GRID_DATA-YNPRCTR.
L_S_YN_20-PERNR    = SY-UNAME.
L_S_YN_20-DVSON    = P_GRID_DATA-YNDVSON.
L_S_YN_20-TGTFLG   = SPACE.
* 2012/04/11 DEL START
*  L_S_YN_20-CSTS     = P_CSTS_1.
* 2012/04/11 DEL END
L_S_YN_20-COMMT    = P_GRID_DATA-YNSGTXT.
L_S_YN_20-YNGJAHR  = LW_YEAR.
L_S_YN_20-BELNR    = P_GRID_DATA-YNBELNR.
L_S_YN_20-BUZEI    = 1.
L_S_YN_20-KNQUAN   = 1.
L_S_YN_20-KNUNIT   = P_GRID_DATA-YNKNUNIT.
* 2012/04/11 MOD START
*  L_S_YN_20-KNUNTPRC = P_GRID_DATA-YNKNUNTPRC.
*  L_S_YN_20-KNUNTPRC = ABS( P_KNETXAMT )."単価は税込絶対値
PERFORM CURRENCY_EXTERNAL USING P_GRID_DATA-YNWAERS
P_KNETXAMT
CHANGING L_S_YN_20-KNUNTPRC.
* 2012/04/11 MOD END
L_S_YN_20-KNTAXAMT = 0.
L_S_YN_20-KNITXAMT = 0.
* 2012/04/11 DEL START
*  L_S_YN_20-KNETXAMT = P_KNETXAMT.
* 2012/04/11 DEL END
* 2012/04/11 ADD START
IF P_MODE = '1'. "売上
L_S_YN_20-CSTS     = P_CSTS_1.
L_S_YN_20-KNETXAMT = P_KNETXAMT.
ELSE.
L_S_YN_20-CSTS     = P_CSTS_2.
L_S_YN_20-KNETXAMT = P_KNETXAMT * -1.
ENDIF.
* 2012/04/11 ADD END

* 2012/04/17 ADD START
*-- 税込みを税抜にコピー
L_S_YN_20-KNITXAMT = L_S_YN_20-KNETXAMT.
* 2012/04/17 ADD END

L_S_YN_20-WAERS    = P_GRID_DATA-YNWAERS.
* 2012/04/11 MOD START
*  IF P_CSTS_1 = C_CSTS_OK.
IF L_S_YN_20-CSTS = C_CSTS_OK.
* 2012/04/11 MOD END
L_S_YN_20-CHKDOC   = P_GRID_DATA-YNCHKDOC.
L_S_YN_20-CHKDAT   = P_GRID_DATA-YNCHKDAT.
L_S_YN_20-CHKUSR   = SY-UNAME.
L_S_YN_20-CZFBDT   = P_CZFBDT.
ELSE.
CLEAR:L_S_YN_20-CHKDOC,
L_S_YN_20-CHKDAT,
L_S_YN_20-CHKUSR,
L_S_YN_20-CZFBDT.
ENDIF.
L_S_YN_20-UPDDAT   = SY-DATUM.
L_S_YN_20-UPDTIM   = SY-UZEIT.
L_S_YN_20-UPDUSR   = SY-UNAME.
L_S_YN_20-UPDPRG   = 'YN010400'.
L_S_YN_20-CKEY1    = P_GRID_DATA-YNCKEY1.
L_S_YN_20-CKEY2    = P_GRID_DATA-YNCKEY2.
L_S_YN_20-LIST1    = P_GRID_DATA-YNLIST1.
L_S_YN_20-LIST2    = P_GRID_DATA-YNLIST2.
L_S_YN_20-LIST3    = P_GRID_DATA-YNLIST3.
L_S_YN_20-LIST4    = P_GRID_DATA-YNLIST4.
L_S_YN_20-LIST5    = P_GRID_DATA-YNLIST5.
L_S_YN_20-LIST6    = P_GRID_DATA-YNLIST6.
L_S_YN_20-LIST7    = P_GRID_DATA-YNLIST7.
L_S_YN_20-LIST8    = P_GRID_DATA-YNLIST8.
L_S_YN_20-INSDT    = SY-DATUM.
L_S_YN_20-LDATE1   = P_GRID_DATA-YNLDATE1.
IF P_KUBUN = C_KUBUN_EXTERNAL.               "外部データの場合
L_S_YN_20-AUTOFLG  = C_KUBUN_MOTOGAIBU.
ELSE.
L_S_YN_20-AUTOFLG  = C_KUBUN_MOTOJISHA.
ENDIF.

INSERT INTO (L_TNAME) VALUES L_S_YN_20.
IF SY-SUBRC <> 0.
ROLLBACK WORK.
RC_CODE = C_RC_CODE_DB_ERROR.
EXIT.
ENDIF.

*-----２明細目
L_S_YN_20-DTLDOC   = L_S_YN_20-DTLDOC + 10000.
L_S_YN_20-BUZEI    = 2.
* 2012/04/11 DEL START
*  L_S_YN_20-CSTS     = P_CSTS_2.
*  LW_KNETXAMT = P_KNETXAMT * -1.
* 2012/04/11 DEL END
* 2012/04/11 ADD START
IF P_MODE = '1'. "売上
L_S_YN_20-CSTS  = P_CSTS_2.
LW_KNETXAMT     = P_KNETXAMT * -1.
ELSE.
L_S_YN_20-CSTS  = P_CSTS_1.
LW_KNETXAMT     = P_KNETXAMT.
ENDIF.
* 2012/04/11 ADD END

* 2012/04/11 MOD START
*  IF P_CSTS_2 = C_CSTS_OK.
IF L_S_YN_20-CSTS = C_CSTS_OK.
* 2012/04/11 MOD END
L_S_YN_20-CHKDOC   = P_GRID_DATA-YNCHKDOC.
L_S_YN_20-CHKDAT   = P_GRID_DATA-YNCHKDAT.
L_S_YN_20-CHKUSR   = SY-UNAME.
L_S_YN_20-CZFBDT   = P_CZFBDT.
ELSE.
CLEAR:L_S_YN_20-CHKDOC,
L_S_YN_20-CHKDAT,
L_S_YN_20-CHKUSR,
L_S_YN_20-CZFBDT.
ENDIF.
L_S_YN_20-KNETXAMT = LW_KNETXAMT .
* 2012/04/17 ADD START
*-- 税込みを税抜にコピー
L_S_YN_20-KNITXAMT = L_S_YN_20-KNETXAMT.
* 2012/04/17 ADD END

INSERT INTO (L_TNAME) VALUES L_S_YN_20.
IF SY-SUBRC <> 0.
ROLLBACK WORK.
RC_CODE = C_RC_CODE_DB_ERROR.
EXIT.
ENDIF.


*----- 処理結果画面用データ
LW_POINT_COMPARE-BUKRS   = P_GRID_DATA-YNBUKRS.
LW_POINT_COMPARE-VRFCTON = P_GRID_DATA-YNVRFCTON.
LW_POINT_COMPARE-BELNR   = P_GRID_DATA-YNBELNR.
APPEND LW_POINT_COMPARE TO GT_POINT_COMPARE.

ENDFORM.                    " INSERT_YN_20_POINT_COMPARA
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  SET_T_ALV_SET_0100
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       部分照合差分結果(差額)の金額変更
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM SET_T_ALV_SET_0100.
DATA:LW_CHANGE_CELL  TYPE LVC_S_MODI.
FIELD-SYMBOLS: <FS> TYPE TYP_GRID_DATA_0100.

LOOP AT GT_CHANGE_CELL INTO LW_CHANGE_CELL.
READ TABLE  T_GRID_DATA_0100 ASSIGNING <FS>
INDEX LW_CHANGE_CELL-ROW_ID.
IF SY-SUBRC = 0.
<FS>-YNKNETXAMT5 = LW_CHANGE_CELL-VALUE.
ENDIF.
ENDLOOP.

ENDFORM.                    " SET_T_ALV_SET_0100
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  PROCESS_EVENT_ENTER_100
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       画面情報リフレッシュ判定
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM PROCESS_EVENT_ENTER_100 .

DATA: L_EVTID TYPE I.
DATA: L_LINES TYPE I.

* Enter押下時に、GT_CHANGE_CELLに値が設定されている場合は
* 画面情報リフレッシュ
IF NOT CL_GUI_ALV_GRID=>CUR_EVENT IS INITIAL.
L_EVTID = CL_GUI_ALV_GRID=>CUR_EVENT->EVENTID.
IF L_EVTID = 19.  " ENTER
DESCRIBE TABLE GT_CHANGE_CELL LINES L_LINES.
IF L_LINES <> 0.
CALL METHOD OBJ_GRID_0100->REFRESH_TABLE_DISPLAY.
CALL METHOD CL_GUI_CFW=>FLUSH.
* 2012/04/11 ADD START
*       チェックボックスが押されたら判定
CLEAR G_CHKBOX_CANGE.
* 2012/04/11 ADD END
ENDIF.
ENDIF.
ENDIF.

* 2012/04/11 ADD START
* チェックボックスが押されたら判定
IF G_CHKBOX_CANGE = C_ON.
CALL METHOD OBJ_GRID_0100->REFRESH_TABLE_DISPLAY.
CALL METHOD CL_GUI_CFW=>FLUSH.
CLEAR G_CHKBOX_CANGE.
ENDIF.
* 2012/04/11 ADD END

ENDFORM.                    " PROCESS_EVENT_ENTER_100
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  GET_VKBUR_NAME
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       営業所名取得
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
*      -->P_DVSON            営業所
*      <--P_DVSONNAME        営業所名
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM GET_VKBUR_NAME USING    P_DVSON
CHANGING P_DVSONNAME.

DATA:LW_VKBUR_NAME TYPE TYP_VKBUR_NAME.

CHECK NOT P_DVSON IS INITIAL.
* 内部テーブルを検索
READ TABLE T_VKBUR_NAME INTO LW_VKBUR_NAME
WITH TABLE KEY VKBUR = P_DVSON.

* すでに取得している場合はこの値を取得
IF SY-SUBRC = 0.
P_DVSONNAME = LW_VKBUR_NAME-BEZEI.
ELSE.
*   まだ取得していない場合は、 ＤＢより取得
SELECT SINGLE
VKBUR
BEZEI
INTO LW_VKBUR_NAME
FROM TVKBT
WHERE SPRAS = C_SPRAS    "言語キー
AND VKBUR = P_DVSON.   "営業所
*   内部テーブルに格納しておく
INSERT LW_VKBUR_NAME INTO TABLE T_VKBUR_NAME.
P_DVSONNAME = LW_VKBUR_NAME-BEZEI.
ENDIF.

ENDFORM.                    " GET_VKBUR_NAME
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  F_READ_TEXT
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       text
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
*      -->P_NAME          READ_TEXT用 NAME
*      -->P_ID            READ_TEXT用 ID
*      -->P_OBJECT        READ_TEXT用 OBJECT
*      <--P_TEXT          READ_TEXTより取得したテキスト(1行目)
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM F_READ_TEXT USING    P_NAME
P_ID
P_OBJECT
CHANGING P_TEXT.

DATA: L_ID      TYPE THEAD-TDID,
L_LANGU   TYPE THEAD-TDSPRAS,
L_NAME    TYPE THEAD-TDNAME,
L_OBJECT  TYPE THEAD-TDOBJECT,
LT_LINES  TYPE STANDARD TABLE OF TLINE,
LW_LINES  TYPE TLINE.

* 汎用モジュール実行可能な属性に変換
L_ID = P_ID.
L_LANGU = C_SPRAS.
L_NAME = P_NAME.
L_OBJECT = P_OBJECT.

* READ_TEXT実行
CALL FUNCTION 'READ_TEXT'
EXPORTING
ID                            = L_ID
LANGUAGE                      = L_LANGU
NAME                          = L_NAME
OBJECT                        = L_OBJECT
TABLES
LINES                         = LT_LINES
EXCEPTIONS
ID                            = 1
LANGUAGE                      = 2
NAME                          = 3
*     NOT_FOUND                     = 4
OBJECT                        = 5
REFERENCE_CHECK               = 6
WRONG_ACCESS_TO_ARCHIVE       = 7
OTHERS                        = 8
.
* 取得できない場合はテキスト初期値
IF SY-SUBRC <> 0.
CLEAR:P_TEXT.
ENDIF.

* 取得したテキストの1行目を返す
READ TABLE LT_LINES INTO LW_LINES INDEX 1.
P_TEXT = LW_LINES-TDLINE.

ENDFORM.                    " F_READ_TEXT
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  CANCEL_DATA_CHECK
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       照合取消 対象データチェック
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM CANCEL_DATA_CHECK.


DATA: LT_CANCEL    TYPE STANDARD TABLE OF TYP_YN10,
LW_CANCEL    TYPE TYP_YN10,
LT_ZN001    TYPE STANDARD TABLE OF TYP_ZN001,
LW_ZN001    TYPE TYP_ZN001,
LT_ZN004    TYPE STANDARD TABLE OF TYP_ZN004,
LW_ZN004    TYPE TYP_ZN004.

* 自社データと外部データを１つにまとめる
APPEND LINES OF T_CANCEL_10 TO LT_CANCEL.
APPEND LINES OF T_CANCEL_20 TO LT_CANCEL.
* 請求先/支払人の重複を削除
SORT LT_CANCEL BY VRFCTON.
DELETE ADJACENT DUPLICATES FROM LT_CANCEL COMPARING VRFCTON.

* 照合期間データ取得

LW_CANCEL-VRFCTON = '+'.
APPEND LW_CANCEL TO LT_CANCEL.
*--- 売上照合処理の場合
IF P_MODE = C_MODE_SALES.
*   照合期間（売上）データ取得
SELECT KUNNR
EDATE
INTO TABLE LT_ZN004
FROM ZN004
FOR ALL ENTRIES IN LT_CANCEL
WHERE KUNNR = LT_CANCEL-VRFCTON.
IF SY-SUBRC = 0.
SORT LT_ZN004.
ENDIF.
*   自社データの照合終了日と、得意先単位での照合終了日を比較
LOOP AT T_CANCEL_10.
READ TABLE LT_ZN004 INTO LW_ZN004
WITH  KEY KUNNR = T_CANCEL_10-VRFCTON
BINARY SEARCH.
IF SY-SUBRC <> 0.
READ TABLE LT_ZN004 INTO LW_ZN004
WITH  KEY KUNNR = '+'
BINARY SEARCH.
ENDIF.
*     照合終了日が同日または、照合終了済みの場合はエラー
IF LW_ZN004-EDATE >= T_CANCEL_10-CZFBDT.
MESSAGE I921.
RC_CODE = C_RC_CODE_ERROR.
EXIT.
ENDIF.
ENDLOOP.

*   外部データの照合終了日と、得意先単位での照合終了日を比較
CHECK RC_CODE = 0.
LOOP AT T_CANCEL_20.
READ TABLE LT_ZN004 INTO LW_ZN004
WITH KEY KUNNR = T_CANCEL_20-VRFCTON
BINARY SEARCH.
IF SY-SUBRC <> 0.
READ TABLE LT_ZN004 INTO LW_ZN004
WITH KEY KUNNR = '+'
BINARY SEARCH.
ENDIF.
*     照合終了日が同日または、照合終了済みの場合はエラー
IF LW_ZN004-EDATE >= T_CANCEL_20-CZFBDT.
MESSAGE I921.
RC_CODE = C_RC_CODE_ERROR.
EXIT.
ENDIF.
ENDLOOP.

*--- 仕入照合処理の場合
ELSE.
*   照合期間（仕入）データ取得
SELECT LIFNR
EDATE
INTO TABLE LT_ZN001
FROM ZN001
FOR ALL ENTRIES IN LT_CANCEL
WHERE LIFNR = LT_CANCEL-VRFCTON.
IF SY-SUBRC = 0.
SORT LT_ZN001.
ENDIF.
*   自社データの照合終了日と、仕入先単位での照合終了日を比較
LOOP AT T_CANCEL_10.
READ TABLE LT_ZN001 INTO LW_ZN001
WITH KEY LIFNR = T_CANCEL_10-VRFCTON
BINARY SEARCH.
IF SY-SUBRC <> 0.
READ TABLE LT_ZN001 INTO LW_ZN001
WITH KEY LIFNR = '+'
BINARY SEARCH.
ENDIF.
*     照合終了日が同日または、照合終了済みの場合はエラー
IF LW_ZN001-EDATE >= T_CANCEL_10-CZFBDT.
MESSAGE I921.
RC_CODE = C_RC_CODE_ERROR.
EXIT.
ENDIF.
ENDLOOP.

*   外部データの照合終了日と、仕入先単位での照合終了日を比較
CHECK RC_CODE = 0.
LOOP AT T_CANCEL_20.
READ TABLE LT_ZN001 INTO LW_ZN001
WITH KEY LIFNR = T_CANCEL_20-VRFCTON
BINARY SEARCH.
IF SY-SUBRC <> 0.
READ TABLE LT_ZN001 INTO LW_ZN001
WITH KEY LIFNR = '+'
BINARY SEARCH.
ENDIF.
*     照合終了日が同日または、照合終了済みの場合はエラー
IF LW_ZN001-EDATE >= T_CANCEL_20-CZFBDT.
MESSAGE I921.
RC_CODE = C_RC_CODE_ERROR.
EXIT.
ENDIF.
ENDLOOP.
ENDIF.

ENDFORM.                    " CANCEL_DATA_CHECK
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       外部データ登録時の伝票以外項目とのデフォルト値
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
