*      <--P_GRID_DATA_0200   外部データ入力ALV構造
*      <--P_SET_WAERS        通貨コード設定フラグ
*      <--P_KNVP             KNVP,KNVV情報
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM GET_DATA3_INIT_LINE USING P_TABIX   TYPE SY-TABIX
CHANGING P_GRID_DATA_0200
TYPE TYP_GRID_DATA_0200
P_SET_WAERS TYPE CHAR01
P_KNVP      TYPE TYP_KNVP_0200.
DATA:LW_YEAR        TYPE GJAHR,       " 会計年度算出用
LW_KUNNR       TYPE CHAR10,      " 得意先内部
LW_ZTERM       TYPE DZTERM,      " 支払条件
LW_ZFBDT       TYPE DZFBDT,      " 計上締日
LW_KNVP        TYPE TYP_KNVP_0200, "支払人取得用
LV_CORD        TYPE KUNNR,         "得意先コード
LV_DAY         TYPE DATUM,         "日付
LV_ZFBDT       TYPE ZFBDT.         "期日計算の支払基準日
DATA:LW_CHANGE_CURRENT  TYPE TYP_CHANGE_CURRENT.
FIELD-SYMBOLS: <FS>.
*** 2012/03/28 INSERT START 1***
DATA : W_YN130 TYPE TYP_YN130,
LW_VRFCTON    TYPE YNLIFNR.      "通貨代表値での検索用
CLEAR:W_YN130,
LW_VRFCTON.
*** 2012/03/28 INSERT END 1***

*** 2012/03/28 DEL START 1***
**-- 照合キー：1 得意先発注番号へコピー
*  P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNCKEY1 = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNLIST2.
**-- 照合キー：2 インボイスNOへコピー
*  P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNCKEY2 = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNLIST8.
*** 2012/03/28 DEL END 1***

**** 2012/07/12 INSERT START ***　登録時支払人初期値でマスタ値提案
**-- 登録かつ支払人初期値の場合、マスタ値提案
*  IF  INPUT_MODE = C_INPUT_MODE_NEW.
*    IF P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNVRFCTON IS INITIAL.
**-- 登録かつ支払人初期値でない場合、何もしない。
**** 2012/07/12 INSERT END ***
* 取引先機能データの取得
LW_KUNNR = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNLIST1+0(10).
CALL FUNCTION 'CONVERSION_EXIT_ALPHA_INPUT'
EXPORTING
INPUT         = LW_KUNNR
IMPORTING
OUTPUT        = LW_KUNNR.
CLEAR:LW_KNVP.
* 受注先に紐づく支払人を取得
READ TABLE T_KNVP INTO LW_KNVP
WITH TABLE KEY KUNNR = LW_KUNNR.
IF SY-SUBRC <> 0.
SELECT SINGLE
KNVP~KUNNR          "得意先コード
KNVP~VKORG          "販売組織
KNVP~VTWEG          "流通チャネル
KNVP~SPART          "製品部門
KNVP~PARVW          "取引先機能
KNVP~PARZA          "取引先カウンタ
KNVP~KUNN2          "取引先の得意先コード
KNVV~WAERS          "通貨コード
KNVV~KALKS          "
INTO LW_KNVP
FROM KNVP INNER JOIN KNVV
ON  KNVP~KUNNR = KNVV~KUNNR
AND KNVP~VKORG = KNVV~VKORG
AND KNVP~VTWEG = KNVV~VTWEG
AND KNVP~SPART = KNVV~SPART
WHERE KNVP~KUNNR = LW_KUNNR
AND KNVP~VKORG = P_VKORG
AND KNVP~VTWEG = P_VTWEG
AND KNVP~SPART = P_SPART
AND KNVP~PARVW = P_PARVWK
AND KNVP~PARZA = SPACE.
IF SY-SUBRC = 0.
INSERT LW_KNVP INTO TABLE T_KNVP.
ENDIF.
ENDIF.
P_KNVP = LW_KNVP.

*** 2012/07/12 INSERT START ***　登録時支払人初期値でマスタ値提案
*-- 登録かつ支払人初期値の場合、マスタ値提案
IF  INPUT_MODE = C_INPUT_MODE_NEW.
IF P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNVRFCTON IS INITIAL.
*-- 登録かつ支払人初期値でない場合、何もしない。
*** 2012/07/12 INSERT END ***

*-- 支払人
P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNVRFCTON = LW_KNVP-KUNN2.
*** 2012/07/12 INSERT START ***　同上
ENDIF.
ENDIF.
*** 2012/07/12 INSERT END ***

*** 2012/07/12 INSERT STRAT ***　受注先に合わせた通貨コード提案
*-- 受注先に合わせた通貨コードの自動提案
IF P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNLIST1 IS INITIAL.
ELSE.
CLEAR LW_KUNNR.
LW_KUNNR = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNLIST1+0(10).
CALL FUNCTION 'CONVERSION_EXIT_ALPHA_INPUT'
EXPORTING
INPUT         = LW_KUNNR
IMPORTING
OUTPUT        = LW_KUNNR.
*-- 通貨換算を実施するため
IF P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNWAERS IS INITIAL.
P_SET_WAERS = C_ON.   "通貨コード設定フラグをON
ENDIF.

SELECT SINGLE WAERS
INTO P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNWAERS
FROM KNVV
WHERE KUNNR = LW_KUNNR
AND VKORG = P_VKORG
AND VTWEG = P_VTWEG
AND SPART = P_SPART.
ENDIF.
*** 2012/07/12 INSERT END
*-- 会計年度(毎回必ず更新)
IF P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNLDATE1 IS INITIAL.
ELSE.
CALL FUNCTION 'BAPI_COMPANYCODE_GET_PERIOD'
EXPORTING
COMPANYCODEID = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNBUKRS
POSTING_DATE  = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNLDATE1
IMPORTING
FISCAL_YEAR   = LW_YEAR.
P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNGJAHR = LW_YEAR.
ENDIF.

*-- 計上締日
*** 2012/03/28 MOD START 2***
*  IF  P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNZFBDT IS INITIAL     "計上締日が未設定
*  AND ( P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNVRFCTON <> SPACE   "支払人が設定
*  AND   P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNLDATE1 <> SPACE ). "検収日が設定
IF  NOT P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNVRFCTON IS INITIAL   "支払人が設定
AND NOT P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNLDATE1  IS INITIAL.  "検収日が設定
*** 2012/03/28 MOD END 2***
LV_CORD = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNVRFCTON.
LV_DAY  = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNLDATE1.
CALL FUNCTION 'YK_ZFBDT_GET_BY_KNVV'
EXPORTING
I_CORD               = LV_CORD
I_VKORG              = P_VKORG
I_VTWEG              = P_VTWEG
I_SPART              = P_SPART
I_DAY                = LV_DAY
I_ZTERM              = SPACE
IMPORTING
E_ZFBDT              = LV_ZFBDT
EXCEPTIONS
NO_GET_T052          = 1
NO_GOOD_GETDAY       = 2
NO_GET_ZTERM         = 3
OTHERS               = 4.
IF SY-SUBRC <> 0.
CLEAR:LV_ZFBDT.
ENDIF.
P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNZFBDT = LV_ZFBDT.
ENDIF.

*** 2012/07/12 DEL START ***　通貨提案削除
**-- 通貨コード(今回設定されたかどうかのフラグも設定)
*  IF      P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNWAERS IS INITIAL
*  AND NOT LW_KNVP-WAERS            IS INITIAL.
*    P_SET_WAERS = C_ON.   "通貨コード設定フラグをON
*  ENDIF.
*  P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNWAERS = LW_KNVP-WAERS.
*** 2012/07/12 DEL END ***

*** 2012/03/28 INSERT START 1***
* 該当レコードの支払人の外部EXIT番号を取得する。
*** 2012/07/12 MOD START ***　EXIT番号の取得方法変更
*  READ TABLE T_YN130 INTO W_YN130
*       WITH KEY VRFCTON = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNVRFCTON
*                BUKRS   = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNBUKRS.
*-- 本時点で、支払人と受注先の紐付けは、崩れている可能性がある。
SELECT SINGLE OUTEXITDOC
INTO W_YN130-OUTEXITDOC
FROM YN130
WHERE VRFCTON = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNVRFCTON
AND BUKRS   = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNBUKRS.
*** 2012/07/12 MOD END ***
IF SY-SUBRC NE 0.
CONCATENATE 'D-' P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNWAERS
INTO LW_VRFCTON.
READ TABLE T_YN130 INTO W_YN130
WITH KEY VRFCTON = LW_VRFCTON
BUKRS   = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNBUKRS.
ENDIF.

IF     W_YN130-OUTEXITDOC = '1001'.
**-- 照合キー：1 得意先発注番号へコピー
P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNCKEY1 = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNLIST2.
CLEAR P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNCKEY2.

ELSEIF W_YN130-OUTEXITDOC = '1002'.
**-- 照合キー：2 インボイスNOへコピー
P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNCKEY2 = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNLIST8.
CLEAR P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNCKEY1.

ELSEIF W_YN130-OUTEXITDOC = '1003'.
**-- 照合キー：1 得意先発注番号へコピー
P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNCKEY1 = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNLIST2.
**-- 照合キー：2 インボイスNOへコピー
P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNCKEY2 = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNLIST8.

ENDIF.
*** 2012/03/28 INSERT END 1***

ENDFORM.                    " GET_DATA3_INIT_LINE
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  INSERT_DATA_INT_LIST1
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       外部データ登録時の受注先/発注先初期値データ
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
*      <--P_YNLIST1          受注先/発注先
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM INSERT_DATA_INT_LIST1 CHANGING P_YNLIST1.

FIELD-SYMBOLS: <FS1>, <FS2>, <FS3>.
DATA: LW_CNT   TYPE I.

LOOP AT P_LIST12.
LW_CNT = LW_CNT + 1.
*   選択画面に入力された1件目のデータを取得
IF LW_CNT = 1.
ASSIGN COMPONENT 1 OF STRUCTURE P_LIST12 TO <FS1>.
ASSIGN COMPONENT 2 OF STRUCTURE P_LIST12 TO <FS2>.
IF <FS2> <> 'CP'.
ASSIGN COMPONENT 3 OF STRUCTURE P_LIST12 TO <FS3>.
P_YNLIST1 = <FS3>.
ENDIF.
*   受注先/発注先に複数入力がある場合は初期提案しない
ELSE.
CLEAR:P_YNLIST1.
ENDIF.
ENDLOOP.

ENDFORM.                    " INSERT_DATA_INT_LIST1
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  CALC_DATA2_INIT_LINE
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*        [売上]外部データ登録時の金額項目デフォルト値編集
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
*      -->P_SET_WAERS        税コード取得フラグ
*      -->P_KNVP             KNVV,KNVP情報
*      <--P_GRID_DATA_0200   外部データ入力ALV構造
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM CALC_DATA2_INIT_LINE    USING P_SET_WAERS TYPE CHAR01
P_KNVP      TYPE TYP_KNVP_0200
CHANGING P_GRID_DATA_0200
TYPE TYP_GRID_DATA_0200.
DATA: LW_TCURX      TYPE TCURX,           " 通貨情報取得要
LW_KINGAKU    TYPE BAPICUREXT,      " 数量×単価計算用
LW_YNKNITXAMT TYPE YNITXAMT,        " 税抜金額(外部表記)
LW_SIGN       TYPE CHAR1,           " 丸めパターン
LW_WRBTR      TYPE WRBTR,           " 属性変換用
LW_TAXKD      TYPE TYP_TAXKD,       " 国コード/税コード取得用
LT_MWDAT      TYPE TABLE OF RTAX1U15," 税額
LW_MWDAT      LIKE LINE  OF LT_MWDAT,
LW_LAND1      TYPE LAND1_GP,         "国コード
L_KSCHL       TYPE A078-KSCHL.       "条件タイプ


*-- 通貨コードが入力されている場合のみ自動計算
CHECK NOT P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNWAERS IS INITIAL.

* 2012/04/18 ADD START
*-- 税抜きと消費税の両方が初期値のときのみ計算処理
IF  P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNKNITXAMT = 0
AND P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNKNTAXAMT = 0.
ELSE.
*-- 税込金額(必ず更新する)
P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNKNETXAMT = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNKNTAXAMT +
P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNKNITXAMT.
EXIT.
ENDIF.
* 2012/04/18 ADD END

*--税抜金額(数量×単価)(未入力の場合に設定)
IF  P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNKNITXAMT = 0
AND ( P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNKNQUAN <> 0
AND   P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNKNUNTPRC <> 0 ).

*   @通貨コードの小数点以下の桁数を取得
READ TABLE T_TCURX INTO LW_TCURX
WITH TABLE KEY CURRKEY = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNWAERS.
IF SY-SUBRC <> 0.
SELECT SINGLE *
INTO LW_TCURX
FROM TCURX
WHERE CURRKEY = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNWAERS.
IF SY-SUBRC = 0.
INSERT LW_TCURX INTO TABLE T_TCURX.
*     取得できない場合は小数桁は２桁をデフォルトとする
ELSE.
LW_TCURX-CURRKEY = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNWAERS.
LW_TCURX-CURRDEC = 2.
INSERT LW_TCURX INTO TABLE T_TCURX.
ENDIF.
ENDIF.

*   A得意先に対する価格決定区分割当を取得
CASE P_KNVP-KALKS.
WHEN '1' OR '4' OR '5'.
LW_SIGN = SPACE.       "四捨五入

WHEN '2' OR '6' OR '7'.
LW_SIGN = '+'.         "切り上げ

WHEN '3' OR '8' OR '9'.
LW_SIGN = '-'.         "切捨て

WHEN OTHERS.
ENDCASE.

*   B数量×単価を算出
LW_KINGAKU = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNKNQUAN *
P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNKNUNTPRC.
CALL FUNCTION 'ROUND'
EXPORTING
DECIMALS            = LW_TCURX-CURRDEC
INPUT               = LW_KINGAKU
SIGN                = LW_SIGN
IMPORTING
OUTPUT              = LW_YNKNITXAMT
EXCEPTIONS
INPUT_INVALID       = 1
OVERFLOW            = 2
TYPE_INVALID        = 3
OTHERS              = 4.
IF SY-SUBRC <> 0.
CLEAR:P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNKNITXAMT.
ENDIF.

*   金額の内部換算
PERFORM CURRENCY_INTERNAL    USING P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNWAERS
LW_YNKNITXAMT
CHANGING P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNKNITXAMT.
ENDIF.

*--消費税額(未入力の場合に設定)
IF  P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNKNTAXAMT = 0         "消費税額 0
AND P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNKNITXAMT <> 0.       "税抜金額 0以外

LW_WRBTR = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNKNITXAMT.     "税抜金額(内部)

*** 2012/03/29 DEL START 1***
*    不要処理なので削除
***  税コードを取得
*    READ TABLE T_TAXKD INTO LW_TAXKD
*         WITH TABLE KEY KUNNR = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNLIST1+0(10).
*
*    IF SY-SUBRC <> 0.
*** 2012/03/29 DEL END 1***

*     @条件タイプの設定
CASE P_KNVP-KALKS.
WHEN '1' OR '2' OR '3'.  "価格のカスタマイズで規定している
L_KSCHL = CNS_MWST.
WHEN '4' OR '6' OR '9'.
L_KSCHL = CNS_MWSU.
WHEN '5' OR '7' OR '8'.
L_KSCHL = CNS_MWSD.
ENDCASE.

*     A受注先をキーに得意先の税分類を取得
SELECT SINGLE
KNA1~LAND1
KNVI~TAXKD
INTO (LW_TAXKD-LAND1,
LW_TAXKD-TAXKD)
FROM KNA1 INNER JOIN KNVI
ON KNA1~KUNNR = KNVI~KUNNR
WHERE KNA1~KUNNR = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNLIST1+0(10)
AND KNVI~ALAND = C_LAND
AND KNVI~TATYP = C_TATYP.

IF  SY-SUBRC = 0.
*** 2012/03/29 MOD START 1***
***      B得意先の国コードが日本の場合
*      IF LW_TAXKD-LAND1 = C_LAND.
*        SELECT KONP~MWSK1
*          INTO LW_TAXKD-MWSK1
*          FROM A002 INNER JOIN KONP
*               ON A002~KNUMH = KONP~KNUMH
*               UP TO 1 ROWS
*          WHERE A002~KAPPL =  P_KAPPL2
*            AND A002~KSCHL =  L_KSCHL
*            AND A002~ALAND =  C_LAND
*            AND A002~TAXK1 =  LW_TAXKD-TAXKD
*            AND A002~TAXM1 =  LW_TAXKD-TAXKD
*            AND A002~DATAB <= P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNLDATE1
*            AND A002~DATBI >= P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNLDATE1.
*        ENDSELECT.
*        IF SY-SUBRC = 0.
*          INSERT LW_TAXKD INTO TABLE T_TAXKD.
*        ENDIF.
*
***       C得意先の国コードが日本以外の場合
*      ELSE.
*        SELECT KONP~MWSK1
*          INTO LW_TAXKD-MWSK1
*          FROM A078 INNER JOIN KONP
*               ON A078~KNUMH = KONP~KNUMH
*               UP TO 1 ROWS
*          WHERE A078~KAPPL =  P_KAPPL2
*            AND A078~KSCHL =  L_KSCHL
*            AND A078~ALAND =  C_LAND
*            AND A078~LLAND =  LW_TAXKD-LAND1
*            AND A078~DATAB <= P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNLDATE1
*            AND A078~DATBI >= P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNLDATE1.
*        ENDSELECT.
*        IF SY-SUBRC = 0.
*          INSERT LW_TAXKD INTO TABLE T_TAXKD.
*        ENDIF.
*      ENDIF.

**      B得意先の国コードが日本以外の場合
IF LW_TAXKD-LAND1 NE C_LAND.
SELECT KONP~MWSK1
INTO LW_TAXKD-MWSK1
FROM A078 INNER JOIN KONP
ON A078~KNUMH = KONP~KNUMH
UP TO 1 ROWS
WHERE A078~KAPPL =  P_KAPPL2
AND A078~KSCHL =  L_KSCHL
AND A078~ALAND =  C_LAND
AND A078~LLAND =  LW_TAXKD-LAND1
AND A078~DATAB <= P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNLDATE1
AND A078~DATBI >= P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNLDATE1.
ENDSELECT.
*** 　　国コードが日本以外であっても検索条件MWSTに準拠し、
***     値が取得できない場合は、テーブル：A002より、値を取得する。
IF SY-SUBRC NE 0.
SELECT KONP~MWSK1
INTO LW_TAXKD-MWSK1
FROM A002 INNER JOIN KONP
ON A002~KNUMH = KONP~KNUMH
UP TO 1 ROWS
WHERE A002~KAPPL =  P_KAPPL2
AND A002~KSCHL =  L_KSCHL
AND A002~ALAND =  C_LAND
AND A002~TAXK1 =  LW_TAXKD-TAXKD
AND A002~TAXM1 =  LW_TAXKD-TAXKD
AND A002~DATAB <= P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNLDATE1
AND A002~DATBI >= P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNLDATE1.
ENDSELECT.
ENDIF.
**      C得意先の国コードが日本の場合
ELSE.
SELECT KONP~MWSK1
INTO LW_TAXKD-MWSK1
FROM A002 INNER JOIN KONP
ON A002~KNUMH = KONP~KNUMH
UP TO 1 ROWS
WHERE A002~KAPPL =  P_KAPPL2
AND A002~KSCHL =  L_KSCHL
AND A002~ALAND =  C_LAND
AND A002~TAXK1 =  LW_TAXKD-TAXKD
AND A002~TAXM1 =  LW_TAXKD-TAXKD
AND A002~DATAB <= P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNLDATE1
AND A002~DATBI >= P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNLDATE1.
ENDSELECT.
ENDIF.
*** 2012/03/29 MOD END 1***
ENDIF.
*** 2012/03/29 DEL START 1***
*    ENDIF.
*** 2012/03/29 DEL END 1***

*   税抜金額分の税額を税コードを使用して算出
IF LW_TAXKD-MWSK1 IS INITIAL.
ELSE.
CALL FUNCTION 'CALCULATE_TAX_FROM_NET_AMOUNT'
EXPORTING
I_BUKRS           = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNBUKRS
I_MWSKZ           = LW_TAXKD-MWSK1
I_WAERS           = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNWAERS
I_WRBTR           = LW_WRBTR
TABLES
T_MWDAT           = LT_MWDAT
EXCEPTIONS
BUKRS_NOT_FOUND   = 1
COUNTRY_NOT_FOUND = 2
MWSKZ_NOT_DEFINED = 3
MWSKZ_NOT_VALID   = 4
KTOSL_NOT_FOUND   = 5
KALSM_NOT_FOUND   = 6
PARAMETER_ERROR   = 7
KNUMH_NOT_FOUND   = 8
KSCHL_NOT_FOUND   = 9
UNKNOWN_ERROR     = 10
ACCOUNT_NOT_FOUND = 11
TXJCD_NOT_VALID   = 12
OTHERS            = 13.
IF SY-SUBRC <> 0.
P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNKNTAXAMT = 0.
ENDIF.

READ TABLE LT_MWDAT INTO LW_MWDAT INDEX 1.
P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNKNTAXAMT = LW_MWDAT-WMWST.
ENDIF.

* 入力した際に通貨コード"JPY"にもかかわらず、内部テーブルの値が
* 円内部換算されないため、内部換算を行う↓↓↓
* 税額に入力がある場合
ELSE.
IF P_SET_WAERS = C_ON.      "今回通貨コードが設定された場合
LW_MWDAT-WMWST = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNKNTAXAMT.
PERFORM CURRENCY_INTERNAL    USING P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNWAERS
LW_MWDAT-WMWST
CHANGING P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNKNTAXAMT.
ENDIF.
ENDIF.

* 税抜き金額に入力があり、今回通貨コードが設定された場合
IF  P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNKNITXAMT <> 0
AND P_SET_WAERS = C_ON.
LW_MWDAT-WMWST = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNKNITXAMT.
PERFORM CURRENCY_INTERNAL    USING P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNWAERS
LW_MWDAT-WMWST
CHANGING P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNKNITXAMT.
ENDIF.
"ここまで↑↑

*-- 税込金額(必ず更新する)
P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNKNETXAMT = P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNKNTAXAMT +
P_GRID_DATA_0200-YNKNITXAMT.

ENDFORM.                    " CALC_DATA2_INIT_LINE
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  F4_VARIANTS
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       バリアント検索ヘルプ
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
*      -->P_HANDLE      画面番号
*      <--P_VARI        バリアント(レイアウト)
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM F4_VARIANTS    USING P_HANDLE
CHANGING P_VARI.

*** 2012/03/07 DEL START １***
*  DATA:LW_VARI   TYPE SLIS_VARI,   "属性変換用
*    LW_PGID TYPE SYREPID.
** PG名コピー
*  LW_PGID = SY-REPID.
*
** ALVバリアントの検索ヘルプ
*  CALL FUNCTION 'SPC_F4_ALV_VARIANTS'
*    EXPORTING
*      PI_RELID              = 'LT'
*      PI_REPORT             = LW_PGID
*      PI_HANDLE             = P_HANDLE
*      PI_LOG_GROUP          = ' '
*      PI_USERNAME           = ' '  "グローバルレイアウト
*    IMPORTING
*      PE_VARIANT            = LW_VARI
*   EXCEPTIONS
*     NO_VALUES_FOUND       = 1
*     OTHERS                = 2.
**
*  IF SY-SUBRC = 0.
*    P_VARI = LW_VARI.
*  ELSE.
*    CLEAR:P_VARI.
*  ENDIF.
*** 2012/03/07 DEL END １***
*** 2012/03/07 INSERT START １***
*-- レイアウト検索ヘルプ乗せ代え
DATA:
LW_DISVARIANT TYPE DISVARIANT.

CLEAR:
LW_DISVARIANT,
P_VARI.

LW_DISVARIANT-REPORT = SY-REPID.
LW_DISVARIANT-HANDLE = P_HANDLE.

CALL FUNCTION 'REUSE_ALV_VARIANT_F4'
EXPORTING
IS_VARIANT         = LW_DISVARIANT
I_SAVE             = C_SAVE
I_DISPLAY_VIA_GRID = C_ON
IMPORTING
ES_VARIANT         = LW_DISVARIANT
EXCEPTIONS
NOT_FOUND          = 1
PROGRAM_ERROR      = 2
OTHERS             = 3.

IF SY-SUBRC = 0.
P_VARI = LW_DISVARIANT-VARIANT.
ENDIF.
*** 2012/03/07 INSERT END １***

ENDFORM.                    " F4_VARIANTS
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  TARGET_DATA_CHECK
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       照合対象のチェック
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM TARGET_DATA_CHECK.
DATA:LT_GRID_DATA_0100  TYPE STANDARD TABLE OF TYP_GRID_DATA_0100,
LS_GRID_DATA       TYPE TYP_GRID_DATA_0100,
LS_GRID_NOT_SELECT TYPE TYP_GRID_DATA_0100,
LW_ERR_FLG         TYPE CHAR1,             "エラーフラグ
LT_YN_20_DATA      TYPE STANDARD TABLE OF TYP_YN_20_DATA,
LS_YN_20_DATA      TYPE TYP_YN_20_DATA.

* チェック用に、一覧データをコピー
LT_GRID_DATA_0100[] = T_GRID_DATA_0100[].
LT_YN_20_DATA[]     = T_YN_20_DATA[].
SORT LT_YN_20_DATA BY YNGJAHR
YNSLPDOC
YNDTLDOC.

* 画面にて、選択されている自社データをループ
LOOP AT T_GRID_DATA_0100 INTO LS_GRID_DATA
WHERE YNCHKBOX = C_ON
AND YNKUBUN  = C_KUBUN_INTERNAL.  "自社データ
CLEAR:LS_GRID_NOT_SELECT.
*   選択されている自社データと同じ伝票番号で選択されていないデータを検索
LOOP AT LT_GRID_DATA_0100 INTO LS_GRID_NOT_SELECT
WHERE YNCHKBOX  = SPACE                    "選択対象外
AND YNGJAHR2  = LS_GRID_DATA-YNGJAHR2    "伝票会計年度
AND YNSLPDOC2 = LS_GRID_DATA-YNSLPDOC2   "伝票番号
AND YNDTLDOC2 <> LS_GRID_DATA-YNDTLDOC2  "伝票明細番号
AND YNCSTS    <> '7'                     "ステータス:自動照合
AND YNCSTS    <> '8'.                    "マニュアル照合

*     YN120/YN220のデータを検索
READ TABLE LT_YN_20_DATA INTO LS_YN_20_DATA
WITH KEY YNGJAHR  = LS_GRID_NOT_SELECT-YNGJAHR2
YNSLPDOC = LS_GRID_NOT_SELECT-YNSLPDOC2
YNDTLDOC = LS_GRID_NOT_SELECT-YNDTLDOC2.
*     部分照合で作成されたデータではない場合、エラー
IF LS_YN_20_DATA-AUTOFLG = SPACE.
LW_ERR_FLG = C_ON.
EXIT.
ENDIF.

ENDLOOP.

*   エラーが発生していない場合は次のレコードへ
IF LW_ERR_FLG = SPACE.
CONTINUE.

*   エラーが発生している場合はメッセージを出力しチェック終了
ELSE.
RC_CODE = C_RC_CODE_ERROR.
MESSAGE I927 WITH LS_GRID_DATA-YNSLPDOC2.
EXIT.
ENDIF.

*   エラーが発生した場合はループ終了
IF RC_CODE = C_RC_CODE_ERROR.
EXIT.
ENDIF.
ENDLOOP.

ENDFORM.                    " TARGET_DATA_CHECK
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  POINT_COMPARE_TARGET_CHECK
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       部分照合対象データチェック
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM POINT_COMPARE_TARGET_CHECK.
DATA:LS_GRID_DATA   TYPE TYP_GRID_DATA_0100,
LW_ERR_FLG     TYPE CHAR1.

* 部分照合のデータのみチェック
LOOP AT T_GRID_DATA_0100 INTO LS_GRID_DATA
WHERE YNTGTFLG = C_ON
AND YNKNETXAMT4 <> 0.

*** 2012/06/04 INSERT START ***
IF P_NOTP = C_ON.
IF LS_GRID_DATA-YNKUBUN = C_KUBUN_EXTERNAL.
IF LS_GRID_DATA-YNKNETXAMT4 NE 0.
MESSAGE I999 WITH '仕入照合の場合、外部データに'
'部分照合残額は入力できません'.
RC_CODE = C_RC_CODE_ERROR.
ENDIF.
ENDIF.
ENDIF.
*** 2012/06/04 INSERT END ***

*--- 税込金額がプラスの場合
IF  ( LS_GRID_DATA-YNKNETXAMT1 > 0    "税込金額(自社)プラス値
AND   LS_GRID_DATA-YNKNETXAMT2 = 0 )
OR  ( LS_GRID_DATA-YNKNETXAMT2 > 0    "税込金額(外部)プラス値
AND   LS_GRID_DATA-YNKNETXAMT1 = 0 ).
*     部分照合残額(入力値)がマイナスはエラー
IF LS_GRID_DATA-YNKNETXAMT4 < 0.
MESSAGE I999 WITH '税込金額が0以上の場合は'
'部分照合残額も0以上の金額を入力してください'.
RC_CODE = C_RC_CODE_ERROR.
EXIT.
ELSE.
*       部分照合残額(入力値)がプラスだが税込金額を上回る場合はエラー
IF (  LS_GRID_DATA-YNKNETXAMT1 < LS_GRID_DATA-YNKNETXAMT4
AND   LS_GRID_DATA-YNKNETXAMT1 > 0 )
OR (  LS_GRID_DATA-YNKNETXAMT2 < LS_GRID_DATA-YNKNETXAMT4
AND   LS_GRID_DATA-YNKNETXAMT2 > 0 ).
MESSAGE I928.
RC_CODE = C_RC_CODE_ERROR.
EXIT.
ENDIF.
ENDIF.

*--- 税込金額がマイナスの場合
ELSE.
*     部分照合残額(入力値)がプラスはエラー
IF LS_GRID_DATA-YNKNETXAMT4 > 0.
MESSAGE I999 WITH '税込金額が0以下の場合は'
'部分照合残額も0以下の金額を入力してください'.
RC_CODE = C_RC_CODE_ERROR.
EXIT.
ELSE.
*       部分照合残額(入力値)がMマイナスだが税込金額を上回る場合はエラー
IF (  LS_GRID_DATA-YNKNETXAMT1 > LS_GRID_DATA-YNKNETXAMT4
AND   LS_GRID_DATA-YNKNETXAMT1 < 0 )
OR (  LS_GRID_DATA-YNKNETXAMT2 > LS_GRID_DATA-YNKNETXAMT4
AND   LS_GRID_DATA-YNKNETXAMT2 < 0 ).
* 2012/04/10 MOD START
*         部分照合残額が、税込金額を下回っています
MESSAGE I941.
* 2012/04/10 MOD END
RC_CODE = C_RC_CODE_ERROR.
EXIT.
ENDIF.
ENDIF.

ENDIF.
ENDLOOP.

ENDFORM.                    " POINT_COMPARE_TARGET_CHECK
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  MAKE_POINT_DATA
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       部分照合BDC用データ編集
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
*      -->P_GRID_DATA     部分照合ALV一覧データ
*      <--P_RATE_FLG      換算レート設定フラグ
*      <--P_KURSF　       換算レート
*      <--P_ZUONR         ソートキー
*      <--P_ZTERM         支払条件
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM MAKE_POINT_DATA USING    P_GRID_DATA TYPE TYP_GRID_DATA_0100
CHANGING P_RATE_FLG  TYPE CHAR1
P_KURSF     TYPE KURSF
P_ZUONR     TYPE DZUONR
P_ZTERM     TYPE DZTERM.
DATA:LW_20_DATA   TYPE TYP_YN_20_DATA,  "YN120/YN220データ構造
LW_DUMMY     TYPE DZUONR.          "ソートキーダミー項目

*----- 換算レート
* 自社データの場合で通貨コードが"JPY"以外の場合に設定
IF  P_GRID_DATA-YNKUBUN = C_KUBUN_INTERNAL
AND P_GRID_DATA-YNWAERS <> 'JPY'.

*   BKPFより換算レートを取得する
SELECT SINGLE KURSF
INTO P_KURSF
FROM BKPF
WHERE BUKRS = P_GRID_DATA-YNBUKRS
AND BELNR = P_GRID_DATA-YNBELNR
AND GJAHR = P_GRID_DATA-YNGJAHR.
*   取得できた場合
IF SY-SUBRC = 0.
*     換算レート設定フラグをONにする
P_RATE_FLG = C_ON.
ENDIF.
ENDIF.

*----- ソートキー/支払条件
IF  P_GRID_DATA-YNKUBUN = C_KUBUN_INTERNAL.
*   YN120/YN220データを検索
READ TABLE T_YN_20_DATA INTO LW_20_DATA
WITH KEY YNGJAHR = P_GRID_DATA-YNGJAHR2
YNSLPDOC = P_GRID_DATA-YNSLPDOC2
YNDTLDOC = P_GRID_DATA-YNDTLDOC2.
*   部分照合の基データが、自動取込で作成されたデータの場合
IF LW_20_DATA-AUTOFLG IS INITIAL.
*     ソートキーの設定
CONCATENATE P_GRID_DATA-YNGJAHR      "会計伝票の会計年度
P_GRID_DATA-YNBELNR      "会計伝票番号
P_GRID_DATA-YNBUZEI      "会計明細番号
INTO P_ZUONR.
*     支払条件の設定
PERFORM GET_BSID_BSIK  USING  P_GRID_DATA-YNBUKRS   "会社コード
P_GRID_DATA-YNGJAHR   "会計年度
P_GRID_DATA-YNBELNR   "伝票番号
P_GRID_DATA-YNBUZEI   "明細番号
P_GRID_DATA-YNVRFCTON "請求先/支払人
CHANGING LW_DUMMY              "ソートキー
P_ZTERM.              "支払条件
*   部分照合の基データが、部分照合で作成されたデータの場合
ELSE.
*     ソートキー支払条件の設定
PERFORM GET_BSID_BSIK  USING  P_GRID_DATA-YNBUKRS   "会社コード
P_GRID_DATA-YNGJAHR   "会計年度
P_GRID_DATA-YNBELNR   "伝票番号
P_GRID_DATA-YNBUZEI   "明細番号
P_GRID_DATA-YNVRFCTON "請求先/支払人
CHANGING P_ZUONR               "ソートキー
P_ZTERM.              "支払条件
ENDIF.

*** 2012/03/10 INSERT START ７***
*** 外部データの場合、仕入は、発注先の支払条件
*** 売上は、支払人の支払条件を適用する。
ELSE.
PERFORM GET_BSID_BSIK_EXTERNAL USING P_GRID_DATA-YNVRFCTON "支払人
P_VKORG               "販売組織
P_VTWEG               "流通ﾁｬﾈﾙ
P_SPART               "製品部門
P_GRID_DATA-YNLIST1   "発注先
P_EKORG               "購買組織
CHANGING P_ZTERM.              "支払条件
*** 2012/03/10 INSERT END ７***
ENDIF.

ENDFORM.                    " MAKE_POINT_DATA
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  GET_BSID_BSIK
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       BSID/BSIKよりソートキー/支払条件取得
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
*      -->P_BUKRS      会社コード
*      -->P_GJAHR      会計伝票の会計年度
*      -->P_BELNR      会計伝票番号
*      -->P_BUZEI      会計伝票の明細番号
*      -->P_VRFCTON    得意先(支払人)/仕入先(請求先)
*      <--P_ZUONR      ソートキー
*      <--P_ZTERM      支払条件
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM GET_BSID_BSIK USING    P_BUKRS    TYPE BUKRS
P_GJAHR    TYPE YNGJAHR
P_BELNR    TYPE YNBELNR
P_BUZEI    TYPE YNBUZEI
P_VRFCTON  TYPE ANY
CHANGING P_ZUONR    TYPE DZUONR
P_ZTERM    TYPE DZTERM.
* 売上照合の場合
IF P_MODE = C_MODE_SALES.
*   BSIDよりデータ取得
SELECT ZUONR
ZTERM
INTO (P_ZUONR,
P_ZTERM)
FROM BSID
UP TO 1 ROWS
WHERE KUNNR = P_VRFCTON  "得意先(支払人)
AND BUKRS = P_BUKRS    "会社コード
AND GJAHR = P_GJAHR    "会計年度
AND BELNR = P_BELNR    "会計伝票番号
AND BUZEI = P_BUZEI.   "会計伝票内の明細番号
ENDSELECT.

* 仕入照合の場合
ELSE.
*   BSIKよりデータ取得
SELECT ZUONR
ZTERM
INTO (P_ZUONR,
P_ZTERM)
FROM BSIK
UP TO 1 ROWS
WHERE LIFNR = P_VRFCTON  "仕入先(請求先)
AND BUKRS = P_BUKRS    "会社コード
AND GJAHR = P_GJAHR    "会計年度
AND BELNR = P_BELNR    "会計伝票番号
AND BUZEI = P_BUZEI.   "会計伝票内の明細番号
ENDSELECT.
ENDIF.

ENDFORM.                    " GET_BSID_BSIK
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  GET_BSID_BSIK_EXTERNAL
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       BSID / BSIK より支払条件を取得する
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
*  -->  P_VRFCTON      支払人
*  -->  P_VKORG        販売組織
*  -->  P_VTWEG        流通チャネル
*  -->  P_SPART        製品部門
*  -->  P_LIST1        発注先
*  -->  P_EKORG        購買組織
*  <--  P_ZTERM        支払条件
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM GET_BSID_BSIK_EXTERNAL USING P_VRFCTON "支払人
P_VKORG   "販売組織
P_VTWEG   "流通チャネル
P_SPART   "製品部門
P_LIST1   "発注先
P_EKORG   "購買組織
CHANGING P_ZTERM.  "支払条件
* 売上照合の場合
IF P_MODE = C_MODE_SALES.
*   VRFCTONを用いて、KNVVよりデータ取得
SELECT SINGLE ZTERM
INTO P_ZTERM
FROM KNVV
WHERE KUNNR = P_VRFCTON  "支払人
AND VKORG = P_VKORG    "販売組織
AND VTWEG = P_VTWEG    "流通チャネル
AND SPART = P_SPART.   "製品部門

* 仕入照合の場合
ELSE.
*   LIST1を用いて、LFM1よりデータ取得
SELECT SINGLE ZTERM
INTO  P_ZTERM
FROM LFM1
WHERE LIFNR = P_LIST1    "発注先
AND EKORG = P_EKORG.   "購買組織
ENDIF.

ENDFORM.                    " GET_BSID_BSIK_EXTERNAL
* 2012/04/11 ADD START
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  CHECK_VBELN_POSNR
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       照合処理：請求明細取りこぼしチェック
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM CHECK_VBELN_POSNR.
DATA:L_T_DATA_0100      TYPE STANDARD TABLE OF TYP_GRID_DATA_0100,
L_W_DATA_0100      TYPE TYP_GRID_DATA_0100,
L_H_GRID_DATA_0100 TYPE TYP_GRID_DATA_0100.

L_T_DATA_0100[] = T_GRID_DATA_0100[].

LOOP AT T_GRID_DATA_0100 INTO L_H_GRID_DATA_0100
WHERE YNTGTFLG =  C_ON
AND AUTOFLG  =  SPACE.  "部分照合で作成されたものでなく
CLEAR:L_W_DATA_0100.
LOOP AT L_T_DATA_0100 INTO  L_W_DATA_0100
WHERE YNGJAHR2  = L_H_GRID_DATA_0100-YNGJAHR2    "伝票会計年度
AND YNSLPDOC2 = L_H_GRID_DATA_0100-YNSLPDOC2   "伝票番号
AND YNSLPDOC2 <> SPACE  "請求伝票番号あり
AND AUTOFLG   =  SPACE  "部分照合で作成されたものでなく
AND YNCSTS    <> '7'    "未照合で
AND YNCSTS    <> '8'    "
AND YNTGTFLG  =  SPACE. "同じ請求番号でチェック無しがあるか？
*     伝票番号 ********** には、他に選択されていない明細があります
MESSAGE I927 WITH L_H_GRID_DATA_0100-YNSLPDOC2.
RC_CODE = C_RC_CODE_ERROR.
EXIT.
ENDLOOP.
IF NOT L_W_DATA_0100 IS INITIAL.
EXIT. "エラー済み
ENDIF.
ENDLOOP.

*  READ TABLE T_GRID_DATA_0100 INTO L_H_GRID_DATA_0100 INDEX 1.

ENDFORM.                    " CHECK_VBELN_POSNR

*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  CURRENCY_EXTERNAL
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       単価の通貨外換算
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM CURRENCY_EXTERNAL USING    P_YNWAERS
P_IN
CHANGING P_OUT.

DATA:LW_BAPICURR TYPE BAPICURR_D,        " 消費税額
LW_CURRENCY TYPE WAERS_CURC,        " 通貨コード
LW_RETURN   TYPE BAPIRETURN.        " リターン

LW_BAPICURR = ABS( P_IN ).
LW_CURRENCY = P_YNWAERS.      "通貨コード

CALL FUNCTION 'BAPI_CURRENCY_CONV_TO_EXTERNAL'
EXPORTING
CURRENCY             = LW_CURRENCY
AMOUNT_INTERNAL      = LW_BAPICURR
IMPORTING
AMOUNT_EXTERNAL      = LW_BAPICURR.

P_OUT = LW_BAPICURR * 1.

ENDFORM.                    " CURRENCY_EXTERNAL

* 2012/04/11 ADD END
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*&      Form  CHECK_DVSON
*&---------------------------------------------------------------------*
*       拠点（営業所・プラント）存在チェック
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
*      -->P_DVSON  拠点（営業所・プラント）存在チェック
*----------------------------------------------------------------------*
FORM CHECK_DVSON USING    P_DVSON
P_VRFCTON
P_BUKRS.

DATA:L_DVSON    TYPE CHAR4.

L_DVSON   = P_DVSON.

CLEAR RC_CODE.
IF P_MODE = C_MODE_SALES.
* 売上の場合は、受注先・営業所で存在チェックを実施
SELECT COUNT(*) INTO COUNTER FROM KNVV  WHERE VKBUR = L_DVSON
AND KUNNR = P_VRFCTON.
ELSE.
SELECT COUNT(*) INTO COUNTER FROM T001K WHERE BWKEY = L_DVSON
AND BUKRS = P_BUKRS.
ENDIF.
IF COUNTER = 0.
RC_CODE = C_RC_CODE_NOT_EXIST.
ELSE.
P_DVSON = L_DVSON.
ENDIF.

ENDFORM.                    " CHECK_DVSON
